# poe-tools — project context

Read this first. Self-hosted Path of Exile 2 (PoE2) browser utility suite: pricing, crafting, rune/drop valuation, and an in-progress gear search. Local-first.
> [!important] **Before ANY Trade2 work, read [RATE-LIMITS.md](RATE-LIMITS.md).** You keep tripping the GGG rate limit (shared IP with prod, burst calls, trusting a stale pre-check) and burning ~9 min each time. The checklist there is non-optional.
> [!session-end] Before ending a session: update the **Where we left off** section below — what changed, what's done vs open, the exact next step. If code changed, commit and push so AGENTS.md and the code stay in sync. This file is the next session's starting point; keep it current.


## Stack
- Zero-dependency Node.js — built-in http/fs/path/child_process only. No framework, no npm deps.
- Single server.js + standalone vanilla HTML/CSS/JS pages (index.html, character-upgrades.html, craft-optimizer.html).
- Run locally: node server.js -> http://127.0.0.1:17777.

## Deploy
- Repo: private GitHub skk-hub/poe-tools.
- Dev on Main PC at C:\Users\User\dev\poe2-craft-pricer-project (dir name differs from deployed name poe-tools).
- Flow: push from PC -> on Docker VM: `git pull && docker compose up -d --build`. The `--build` is MANDATORY: the image bakes ALL files via `COPY . .`, so without a rebuild the container keeps serving stale assets. (2026-06-14: removed the old partial bind-mounts that only live-updated server.js + index.html — they masked staleness: a `git pull` without `--build` refreshed those two files while theme.css/tool-css/tool-js/fonts stayed at the last build, serving a half-new, UNSTYLED site. Image is now the single source of truth.)
- Runtime state is NOT in the image (it's `.dockerignore`d). It's written to `DATA_DIR=/app/data` on the named volume `poe-data` (compose), so a `--build` redeploy — which recreates the container and drops its writable layer — does NOT wipe the rolling economy-history graph, caches, or Trade2 rate-limit safety state. Code stays baked in the image (single source of truth); only mutable state is mounted. Locally `DATA_DIR` is unset → falls back to repo ROOT (unchanged). All 9 `.json` state files go through `path.join(DATA_DIR, …)` in server.js; web assets still use ROOT.
- Runs as container poe-tools on :17777. Access: LAN REDACTED-LAN-HOST:17777; Tailscale docker:17777.
- Monitor: Uptime Kuma HTTP check on /api/trade-status (no external calls).
- **VPN (2026-06-23): poe-tools routes through a `gluetun` NordVPN sidecar** so the app's GGG calls exit on a Nord IP, SEPARATE from the home IP the user's game client uses — so the user's in-game trading no longer shares/trips the rate-limit budget with the app. (This is escaping the contended shared IP with ONE dedicated IP — NOT rotation/evasion, rotation was considered and rejected as ban-risky.) Compose: `vpn` (qmcgaw/gluetun, NET_ADMIN + /dev/net/tun) connects via NordVPN **OpenVPN service credentials**; poe-tools uses `network_mode: "service:vpn"` and the `17777` port is published on the `vpn` container (not poe-tools — can't have both ports + network_mode). **`.env` (gitignored) next to docker-compose.yml is now REQUIRED**: `NORD_USER`/`NORD_PASS` (Nord dashboard → "Set up NordVPN manually" → Service credentials, NOT email/pw) + optional `NORD_COUNTRY` (default Netherlands, keep EU for the EU realm). `.env.example` is the template. `FIREWALL_OUTBOUND_SUBNETS=REDACTED-LAN-NET/24,REDACTED-CGNAT-RANGE/10` keeps LAN + Tailscale inbound working. **Deploy order matters**: set `.env` on the VM FIRST, then `docker compose up -d --build` — if gluetun can't auth, poe-tools has no network (killswitch) and the app is unreachable. **Test after**: `docker exec poe-vpn wget -qO- https://api.ipify.org` (should show the Nord IP, not home), then confirm LAN/Tailscale still reach :17777 and a tab read works (Cloudflare may block some Nord OpenVPN IPs — if reads 403, change `NORD_COUNTRY`/server). **Revert** if it breaks access: `git revert` the compose change (back to direct `ports: 17777` + no vpn) and redeploy. The browser-side paste read (prior entry) still exists as a no-VPN fallback.
- **VPN country selector (top bar, 2026-06-28):** the appbar has a `.vpnpill` country dropdown (`#vpnSelect`) that switches the exit country **live, no redeploy**. It hits `server.js` `GET/POST /api/vpn`, which talks to gluetun's **control server** on `127.0.0.1:8000` (reachable because poe-tools shares the vpn netns). GET → `/v1/publicip/ip` (shows current country/city/ip + the curated EU `VPN_COUNTRIES` list); POST → `PUT /v1/vpn/settings` `{provider:{server_selection:{countries:[c]}}}` — gluetun's `SetSettings` auto-cycles Stopped→Running on change, so the tunnel reconnects to the new country (no manual status cycle). The UI then polls `/api/vpn` (~45s) until the country changes. **Requires `gluetun-auth.toml`** (bind-mounted to `/gluetun/auth/config.toml`): current gluetun needs control-server auth, so it opens just those two routes `auth="none"` (control port isn't published → local-netns only). The pill **hides itself** when gluetun is unreachable (local dev), so it only appears on the VPN'd container. `NORD_COUNTRY` is now just the BOOT default; a `docker compose up` recreate resets to it. `GLUETUN_URL` env overrides the control-server base. Couldn't live-test (no gluetun locally) — verified the API shape against gluetun source (`internal/vpn/state/vpn.go` SetSettings, `internal/configuration/settings` json tags) + screenshot of the pill; confirm on the VM that a switch actually reconnects.

## Data sources
- **PRIMARY = poe.ninja, via Exiled-Exchange-2's proxy (ban REVERSED 2026-06-27).** EE2's authoritative value comes from poe.ninja (`PriceTrend.vue` → `usePoeninja()`); our Trade2-bulk reads were genuinely worse (Masterwork Rune: bulk floor 1 div vs real **0.25 div**; Celestial Alloy bulk 20ex vs real **256ex**). User lifted the ban. `getProxyData(league)` fetches **`api.exiledexchange2.dev/proxy/league/overviewData.json`** (EE2's proxy — NOT poe.ninja directly; poe.ninja's API is still CF-blocked server-side, 404). ONE cached fetch (`.ee2-proxy.json`, 25-min TTL) → every item's divine value + 30d volume, **zero GGG rate-limit exposure**. `core.rates.exalted`=divineEx; per-item `primaryValue`×divineEx=ex. `proxyPrice(proxy,name)` looks it up. `parseProxyOverview` + `ee2-proxy-test.js`. Keep usage light (it's EE2's infra). `EE2_PROXY_BASE` env overrides the URL. See memory [[no-poe-ninja-ever]] (now "poe.ninja is primary").
- **GGG Trade2 bulk exchange (`exchangePriceEx`/`ee2SidePrices`) is now SECONDARY:** (a) the **live buyable offers** shown beside each Rune Picker value (the `sideLine`, e.g. "1 div ×92 · 1 ex ×1"), and (b) the **fallback** when the proxy is unreachable. Per-item, single-offer cheapest per side, qty as `minimum`, lone-bait drop, cached in `.ee2-prices.json`. So the Rune Picker shows **value (poe.ninja) + live offers (Trade2)** — like EE2's two panels. Currency strip (`fetchExchangeData`) + economy chart (`economyCurrent`) also price off the proxy first, bulk/cluster fallback.
- Illiquid high-value items (omens, Hinekora's): priced off the DIVINE side of the exchange via `divineMarketPrice` (cheapest *clustered* offer — robust to lowball bait + lone walls). Mirror isn't on the exchange (one price wall), so it's not sampled; would need Trade2 item-search to add.

## Tools — status
- SPA shell (2026-06-14): index.html is the WHOLE app and is now SHELL-ONLY (~570 lines = `<head>` links + view markup + a tiny routing `<script>`). Every tool is a true inline `data-view` view (no iframes), each split into its own files: **`<tool>.css`** (`arbitrage.css`, `map-juicer.css`, `gear-search.css`, `rune-picker.css`, all prefix-scoped under `.toolroot-<x>`) + **`<tool>.js`** (`arbitrage.js`, `map-juicer.js`, `gear-search.js`, `rune-picker.js`, `craft-pricer.js`, `craft-pricer.css`; `home.js` powers the home currency strip; `waystone-data.js` is Map Juicer's data dep). What stays inline in index's `<style>` is home/hub CSS **plus a genuinely-shared tool-view baseline** (`input`/`button`/`textarea`/`.pagehead`/`.sub`/`.controls`/`.status`/`.tablewrap`/`table`/`.muted`) that arb/gear/map reuse via unscoped selectors — it stays in index because the cascade is theme→arb→map→gear→rune→index `<style>` (index last), and moving the baseline to theme.css would flip arb's `.tablewrap` override. Tools: Home (markup + `home.js` currency strip), Craft Pricer (BLANKED placeholder — pending a full reimagining; nav link + `#craft-pricer` view show a `.rebuild-note`, no `#cpGrid`/controls; `craft-pricer.js`/`.css` stay LINKED and the CRAFTS data is preserved for the rebuild, JS no-ops with no DOM), Rune Picker, Gear Search, Map Juicer, Arbitrage — hash-routed under one shared header/nav. (2026-06-14: removed the "More Tools"/`coming-soon` view + nav link + hero button and the hallucinated placeholder cards — Farming Notes/Currency Watchlist/Craft Planner/Profit Notes — per user; they were invented, not real tools.) Collision-safety: tool CSS is **prefix-scoped** (`.toolroot-<x> …`, browser-portable — was `@scope`, converted for old-browser support); tool JS is a `window.__viewInit["<view>"]=function(){…}` lazy fn (function scope isolates the shared globals `esc/els/render/setStatus/fmt` AND defers network to first open). Arbitrage's colliding IDs were renamed `#status/#results/#summary`→`#ab*`. The shell's `showView()` calls `runViewInit(key)` (fires each view's init once) + a DOMContentLoaded re-run for direct-hash loads. Standalone `arbitrage-scanner.html`/`waystone-juicer.html`/`character-upgrades.html` are thin REDIRECTS to `index.html#<view>`. **To add/edit a tool:** its `<tool>.css` (prefix every selector with `.toolroot-<x>`), its `<tool>.js` (wrap in `window.__viewInit["<view>"]=function(){…}`), a `<section class="view toolroot-<x>" id="<view>" data-view="<view>">` in index, a nav link, and the `<link>`+`<script src>`. Then `node smoke-test.js`.

## Gear Upgrade Finder — WORKING (PoB-driven, 2026-06-26)
Import your real PoB build → pick a slot → get upgrades ranked by **real headless-PoB DPS/EHP**. Flow evolved a lot this session; **current shape**: Analyze a slot (headless perturbation → per-stat weights for YOUR build; build-aware payoff: a capped resist scores ~0, an under-cap one scores high — Ammyproper helmet: fireRes ×20, capped cold/light dropped), then **three ways to act**: (1) **"Rank by real DPS"** [PRIMARY] — fetch a batch of in-budget candidates + score each in PoB + sort by ACTUAL ΔDPS; (2) **paste an item** → exact ΔDPS/ΔEHP (pure headless, no trade); (3) a **build-weighted trade search** [secondary, under a toggle] you run in your logged-in browser via a one-time bookmarklet. The weighted *sum* is a linear heuristic and surfaced DPS downgrades (it can't see attack-speed × flat-damage multiplication) — that's why real-DPS rank + paste-to-score became primary.
- **Headless spike PASSED (the gate).** `pob-bridge.lua` (vendored, adapted from PoB's `HeadlessWrapper.lua`) runs PoB-PoE2 headless under **LuaJIT** (installed via `winget DEVCOM.LuaJIT` → `C:\Users\User\AppData\Local\Programs\LuaJIT\bin\luajit.exe`), stubbing SimpleGraphic. It loads a build XML and computes stats that **match PoB exactly** (Ammyproper.xml: Life 1735, ES 2038, EHP 23451, res — and TotalDPS 0, which is correct: that build's own saved `<PlayerStat>` records 0, it has no active skill). Item what-if via PoB's own misc calculator (`GetMiscCalculator` → `{repSlotName, repItem}`), proven non-destructive: swapping a ring moves EHP/res.
- **`pob.js`** (zero-dep, `child_process`): spawns ONE persistent luajit subprocess speaking a length-framed stdio protocol (READY sync sentinel; **payload normalized to LF — Windows text-mode stdin collapses CRLF and would hang the byte-count read**). `available()` (graceful-absent → tool would fall back to stat-only, but headless is present here), `load(xml)`, `calc(slot,itemText)`. PoB slot names key the calc (`toolSlotToPob`: ring1→"Ring 1", chest→"Body Armour", bow→"Weapon 1", quiver→"Weapon 2").
- **Endpoints (server.js, zero new deps — `zlib`+`Buffer`+regex):** `GET /api/gear/builds`; `POST /api/gear/import` ({code}=base64url+zlib.inflate, {buildFile}=basename-guarded, or **{xml}**=a build saved in the browser → `parsePobBuild`: `<Item>` text→`parseItemStats`, `<Slot>`→slot ids, `<PlayerStat value stat>` value-FIRST); `POST /api/gear/weights` (headless perturbation: `computeGearWeights` appends each rollable stat's `GEAR_PROBE_TEMPLATES` mod-line to the current item, recomputes, `weight=Δmetric/increment`, metric=DPS else EHP, normalized 1–20; also returns a weighted `type:"weight"` query); `POST /api/gear/realrank` ({buildXml,slot,mods,maxPriceDiv} → 1 stat-min search + 1 fetch, then `pobItemFromTradeEntry` formats each fetched item, headless-scores it, sorts by ΔDPS — the accurate ranker; **stat mins floored at 70% of your current rolls, not 100%** — requiring ≥ current returned ZERO candidates on near-BIS items even at huge budgets, the empty-state wrongly blamed the budget; PoB ΔDPS sorts the wider net honestly); `POST /api/gear/score` (paste-to-score: headless ΔDPS/ΔEHP for pasted items, **no trade**; falls back to `reconstructItem` grafting when the paste has no base); `POST /api/gear/basic-link` (1 anon search → shareable URL). **RETIRED `/api/gear/search`+`/api/gear/rank`** (old fetch-and-score). **Trade query note: a `type:"count"` stat-group is FINE on PoE2 trade **as long as it carries a `value` (e.g. `value:{min:1}`)** — VERIFIED LIVE 2026-07-01 (an amulet `count` group OR-ing explicit+implicit rarity ≥20 returned 100 results; a combined and+count query also 200s). Use it to OR stats across affix types (that's how the "Require Item Rarity" floor now catches Gold Amulet's implicit rarity — see `injectRarityGroup`). The earlier "count 400s" claim was wrong (likely a value-less group).** (Also: the API hashes a query to a deterministic search id; POSTing the SAME query many times fast soft-400s — a testing artifact, not a real-usage problem.)
- **SPA `gear-finder` view** (`gear-finder.css`/`.js`, nav "Gear Finder", `toolroot-gear`): **My-builds dropdown** (named saves in `localStorage` `poe2.gearFinder.builds` — the VM's PoB-folder picker is empty, so this is how you avoid re-pasting; "Save this build as …" after import) + paste-code import; build-summary tiles; slot chips; budget; **Analyze slot** → weight bars; **Rank by real DPS** (primary); **paste-an-item → exact gain** box; and a collapsible weighted-search (Copy search + a one-time **bookmarklet** "⚡ PoB Trade Search" you drag to bookmarks — reads the copied query off the clipboard and POSTs it in your logged-in pathofexile.com session; console-snippet fallback). Verified headless-shell: import/saves/weights/paste-score all work, 0 console errors. smoke **119/0**.
- **Robustness fixes this session:** (a) **A bad/odd item used to crash PoB's calc and POISON the persistent process** (every later item then failed) — `pob-bridge.lua` now validates the item has a `base` BEFORE calcing; bad paste → clean error, process stays healthy. (b) **Trade-site copies omit the item name + base type** (they start at the item class) and PoB can't read a baseless item → paste-to-score grafts the pasted mods onto your CURRENT item's base (`reconstructItem`; DPS accurate, EHP approximate, flagged "base assumed"). `pobItemFromTradeEntry` (API-fetched items DO carry the base) formats cleanly for realrank.
- **OPEN / untested-live:** **`/api/gear/realrank` end-to-end** (search→fetch→score) is code-validated piece-by-piece (query 200 via direct fetch; fetched-item format scores in PoB; gates on `limited`) but NOT run fully live — I rate-limited the Main-PC IP spamming the same test query. The **VM's dedicated VPN IP is separate**, so the user tests it fresh; if the first realrank/basic-link query errors, tweak the `and`/category shape. The **weighted snippet's live ranking** is also unverifiable by us (weighted POST 400s anonymously — runs in the user's session); confirm + adjust `buildWeightedGearQuery` (`weight`/`sort`) if needed.
- **Split-host setup (the app runs on the VM, PoB lives on the Main PC).** Headless PoB can only run where PoB+LuaJIT are installed = the Main PC, but the app runs in Docker on the VM. Bridge: **`pob-agent.js`** — a tiny zero-dep HTTP server you run on the PC (`node pob-agent.js`, default `:17778`, LAN/Tailscale only) that exposes `/pob/health|load|calc` via local `pob.js`. **`pob.js` has a remote mode**: set **`POB_BRIDGE_URL=http://<pc-lan-or-tailscale-ip>:17778`** on the VM and the VM's server proxies `load`/`calc` to the PC agent (`available()` optimistic, `ready()` = async health check feeding the UI badge). The VPN sidecar doesn't intercept this — LAN/Tailscale subnets are in `FIREWALL_OUTBOUND_SUBNETS`. Verified locally (agent on :17778 + server with `POB_BRIDGE_URL` → `/api/gear/weights` returns identical weights via proxy). So: run `pob-agent.js` on the PC while using Gear Finder; without it (or `POB_BRIDGE_URL` unset / agent down) the VM shows "Stat-only". The agent MUST NOT have `POB_BRIDGE_URL` in its own env (it refuses, to avoid self-proxy). Run it under **pm2** (user already uses pm2): `pm2 start ecosystem.config.js && pm2 save` — `ecosystem.config.js` configures the `pob-agent` app with autorestart + blanks `POB_BRIDGE_URL` (forces local mode). Note: it keeps PoB resident in RAM on the gaming PC, so don't boot-autostart it if you'd rather start it on-demand. Local-only use still works with zero config (no `POB_BRIDGE_URL` → local spawn). `POB_LUAJIT`/`POB_DIR`/`POB_BUILDS_DIR` env-overridable. **CONFIRMED WORKING on the VM (2026-06-26)** after three gotchas: (1) PC↔VM are on different LAN subnets (PC `192.168.100.x`, VM `10.10.10.x`) → must use the PC's **Tailscale** IP (`REDACTED-TAILNET-IP-B`), which is inside `FIREWALL_OUTBOUND_SUBNETS` (`REDACTED-CGNAT-RANGE/10`); (2) the PC's Windows Firewall already allowed it (node.exe inbound on the Private profile, Tailscale interface = Private — no rule needed); (3) **the Tailscale ACL is default-deny** — had to add `tcp:17778` to the `docker → main` grant (the PoB-agent port). `POB_BRIDGE_URL` is wired through `docker-compose.yml` so the VM side is one `.env` line.

### Original scope (kept for the rebuild)
Approved scope:
- Free-form gear import -> slot-aware filters -> budget -> Trade2 query preview -> first 20 listings -> full current-vs-candidate stat comparison.
- Build the shared adaptive Trade2 queue FIRST (trade-queue.js), then build Gear Search on top.
- No result cache. Persistent safety state only.
- Out of scope for v1: OAuth, guide logic, scoring, multi-slot scans.

## Conventions
- **RESTART the local server after editing `.env` or when values look stale.** `server.js` reads `.env` (incl. `POESESSID`) **ONCE at startup** (the zero-dep loader at the top), so a changed `POESESSID`/`EE2_PROXY_BASE`/etc. does NOTHING until you stop and re-run `node server.js`. The server also spawns ONE persistent headless-PoB subprocess (via `pob.js`) that loads PoB's data once and stays resident — if PoB itself updated (a patch) or the build values seem stale, restart the server to respawn it. **Split-host (VM uses the PC's PoB):** restart `pob-agent.js` too (`pm2 restart pob-agent`) — it keeps PoB resident on the PC. Kill stray `node server.js` first (see the zombie-server gotcha) so you don't keep talking to an old instance with old env. (If a fresh `POESESSID` "isn't working", 99% of the time the server wasn't restarted.)
- **ALWAYS push code changes immediately after making them — never leave them only local.** The VM deploys from `origin` (`git pull && docker compose up -d --build`), so an unpushed change is undeployable and the next session/the VM sees stale code. Edit → smoke-test → `git commit && git push` in the same session, every time. (This is the standing rule, not just a session-end nicety.)
- **RUN `pm2 restart pob-agent` YOURSELF whenever a change needs it — do NOT tell the user to do it (user directive 2026-06-29: "no reason not to").** The pob-agent runs under pm2 on the Main PC = THIS box, so you can just run it. Restart it when: (a) you edited `pob-bridge.lua` or `pob-agent.js` (e.g. new STAT_KEYS) — the resident PoB won't pick up changes until reloaded, and the failure is SILENT (partial/missing stats); (b) the agent's resident stats look stale or over-read (it drifts from a fresh calc — observed serving Fire 75/Rarity 80 while a fresh load gives the real 68/73, which broke the Set Optimizer's breakpoint defaults). Do it as part of the closing step alongside commit+push, then confirm with `pm2 list` (status `online`, restart count bumped). Server.js/client-only changes do NOT need it (VM auto-deploys those), but when in doubt a restart is harmless.
- **Run `node smoke-test.js` after any UI/shell change.** 28 checks: pages/scripts parse, no @scope/iframe/token-cycle regressions, redirects, deep-link view init, 0 console errors, 0 overflow (desktop+mobile), a11y focus/announce, and the data-table styling (via mocked rows). Zero-dep static+HTTP checks always run; browser checks auto-find Playwright+Chromium (npx cache or global) and skip — never fail — if absent. Exit !=0 on failure. Proven to catch the deep-link regression (negative-control tested).
- **Browser verification must stay SILENT (no focus-stealing window) — but it's allowed.** The user wants full capability; they just don't want a window popping up and stealing focus from their game. Full `chrome.exe` — even headless — flashes a focus-stealing window on Windows; the **`chrome-headless-shell.exe`** binary is genuinely windowless. `smoke-test.js`'s `chromiumExe()` now PREFERS the headless-shell, so `node smoke-test.js` runs the browser checks silently — no window, no focus steal (verified 2026-06-24). So: prefer `curl`/API probes + reading code for most checks (faster), and use the browser when a visual/interaction check genuinely needs it — just make sure any Playwright launch uses the headless-shell `executablePath` (mirror `chromiumExe()`), never full `chrome.exe`. `SMOKE_NO_BROWSER=1 node smoke-test.js` still exists to skip browser checks entirely if ever needed, but it's no longer required. **A VISIBLE / non-headless browser (e.g. the real Chrome via claude-in-chrome) IS allowed when a task genuinely needs it (e.g. a site like poe2db that bot-blocks the headless-shell) — but ASK THE USER FIRST and get approval before opening it, every time (user directive 2026-07-01). Default stays the windowless headless-shell; the visible browser is opt-in, per-task, on request.**
- Keep every tool dependency-free and local-first.
- ALL trade2 API calls go through the shared persistent adaptive queue. Never call trade2 directly.
- **Trade2 testing discipline (don't over-limit yourself):** the user WANTS live verification, not skipped tests out of caution. Before any live Trade2 call, GET `/api/trade-status` and check `limited`/`secondsRemaining`/the `rateLimit` rule states FIRST; if clear, make the spaced live calls you need; if `limited`, wait the cooldown or use `previewOnly`. Check the limit, don't avoid the API. (See memory `dont-trade-limit-during-testing`.)
- **Record/replay = develop + test with ZERO live GGG calls (the legit answer to "testing trips the limit" — NOT IP rotation/evasion, which stays declined as ban-risky).** Implemented in `trade-queue.js` (the single chokepoint — ALL Trade2 incl. exchange/data/static goes through `tradeQueue.request`). `POE_RECORD=1 node server.js` → every real response is captured to `trade-fixtures.json` keyed by sha1(method+path+body). `POE_OFFLINE=1 node server.js` → serves those fixtures back, never touching the network or the rate-limit budget; `/api/trade-status` reports `replay:true, limited:false`; a fixture MISS throws (graceful `found:false` at the endpoints, never a silent live call). To capture fixtures: when the limit is quiet, `POE_RECORD=1 node server.js`, exercise the tool through the UI once (each unique request is recorded), stop, commit `trade-fixtures.json`. Then all later dev/smoke runs use `POE_OFFLINE=1` and never spend budget. The search `id` lives in the recorded search response, so a replayed search→fetch chain stays consistent. Self-check: `node trade-queue-test.js`.
- **NEVER raw-curl pathofexile.com — route EVERY call through `trade-queue.js`.** This includes the data endpoints `data/filters`, `data/items`, `data/stats` — they are rate-limited too and DON'T pre-warn. Raw `curl` bursts bypass the 3s spacing AND don't record the block in `.trade-status.json`, so they trip the shared IP and the queue can't even see it. For one-off probes write a tiny throwaway node script that uses `createTradeQueue` (statusFile `.trade-status.json`), make calls sequentially through `q.request`, then delete it. One call at a time, spaced. Do NOT fire parallel curls "just to look something up". (You have tripped this repeatedly — stop.)
- UI: premium dark dashboard. Shared design system in **theme.css** (linked first on every page) is the single source of color/type/spacing/radius/shadow/motion tokens — set tokens there, not per-page. v2 direction: NEUTRAL charcoal surfaces (near-black, ~0 chroma — never brown), gold strictly a sparse accent, real radii + soft layered shadows. Type: **Inter for ALL UI/headings/nav/buttons AND the brand wordmark** (Cinzel retired 2026-06-25 — looked dated; `--font-display` now aliases `--font-ui`, the cinzel.woff2 @font-face is dead/unfetched); JetBrains Mono for data. Brand mark is an inline SVG gem in the gold tile (not a letter, not the copyrighted PoE2 logo). Reusable components: `.btn`(+`-primary`/`-ghost`/`-sm`), `.badge`(+`-live`), `.card`/`.panel`, `.field`. theme.css also carries a scoped (`.appbar`/`.bar`) modern header + responsive nav that overrides per-page styles. CRITICAL: never alias a primary token to itself (e.g. `--gold:var(--gold)`) — it creates a CSS cycle that blanks the token. Pages keep only page-specific layout in their inline `<style>`; do NOT re-declare `:root` tokens.
- Primary author: Codex (on Main PC).

## Gotchas (landmines — read before touching pricing / market probes / UI)
- **The in-game price-check LIES for multi-mod items.** It prices off a handful of thin/aspirational *exact-match* listings, so it can read 10x+ the real liquid value. Verified live: juiced corrupted maps the overlay called "40–70ex" / "2 div" **sold for 5ex instantly**. Never quote the overlay as truth — trust the buy-side floor (cheapest real ask) or a confirmed sale.
- **Gate market probes on the ACTUAL item class.** A naive `sort:price asc` "cheapest at threshold" search returns junk (non-corrupted, low-roll, unjuiced) and badly under-prices. For waystones, gate on **corrupted (`misc_filters.corrupted.option:"true"`) + 0 revives (`map_filters.map_revives.max:0`)** to price the class the user actually has. This single mistake produced three wrong conclusions this session before it was caught.
- **Waystone value is COMBINATION-driven, not per-stat.** A single high stat is ~5ex bulk *even at max roll* (Monster Rarity ≥75 alone = 1–5ex, Drop ≥110 alone = 1ex). The chase is (a) Item Rarity ≥60% (~50–180ex, scarce; ≥70% doesn't exist), or (b) high-roll combos that all carry **Drop Chance ≥100%** (`monrar≥70+drop≥100+pack≥25` = 25/100/400ex). Per-stat curves can't express combos — `buildDump` keys on the combo signals, not a value sum. Drop ≥100% is also a real game breakpoint (guaranteed extra drops/pinnacle shards) and the user's "never trash >100%" keep-rule.
- **[OBSOLETE 2026-06-27 — the bid book + `refreshRuneBook`/`cheapestAsk`/`robustBidPx` were DELETED with Tab Tracker.]** The Rune Picker prices like Exiled-Exchange-2 now (cheapest single-offer ask per side, see "latest 31"); there is no bid book / "no buyers" / item-search fallback anymore. Historical detail lived here about par-spam, de-bait, page-cap starvation, and chase-item item-search — all gone with the code. If rune pricing needs work, it's `exchangePriceEx`/`ee2SidePrices`, not a book.
- **The Trade2 SEARCH endpoint (`/search` + `/fetch`) is on a MUCH tighter rate policy than the bulk exchange.** A few searches in a row trip it where the same number of exchange calls is fine. So: never burst searches, and budget any item-search hard. The bulk exchange is cheap; search is precious.
- **`trade-queue.js` paces PROACTIVELY to avoid bans — do NOT cap the gap below a rule's sustainable rate.** GGG's IP rules `[5,15,60] [10,90,300] [30,300,1800]` mean the `[30,300]` rule needs ~10s/call SUSTAINED; the `[…,1800]` is a **30-min ban** if you exceed 30 req/5min. `tuneGap` holds `interval/limit` (+12% headroom) once ≥50% of a rule's budget is used, brakes harder at ≤2 left, and caps a single wait at **120s** (was 30s — the old 30s cap GUARANTEED a trip on the `[30,300]` rule and caused the "1h for 9 items" bug). Bursts stay fast for small ops; big runs (a 233-item tab ≈ 32 calls) auto-throttle to ~7min and never ban. If you change pacing, simulate against those exact rules first (a fresh throwaway, like the one in the 2026-06-25 commit) — this is the SHARED queue, every tool rides it.
- **NEVER launch full `chrome.exe` for browser checks — even headless it flashes a focus-stealing window on Windows** (yanks the user out of their game). Use Playwright's **`chrome-headless-shell.exe`** (truly windowless); `smoke-test.js` `chromiumExe()` already prefers it. Any ad-hoc Playwright must set `executablePath` to the headless-shell too. `SMOKE_NO_BROWSER=1 node smoke-test.js` skips browser checks entirely.
- **On-volume caches survive `--build`** (the named volume isn't rebuilt), so a stale cache can silently defeat a fix. The EE2 price cache `.ee2-prices.json` is TTL'd (15 min) so it self-heals; if a pricing change must invalidate it immediately, delete the file on the volume or change its key shape.
- **Rune/exchange items resolve to one of: priced · "no buyers" (thin) · "pricing…" (not booked yet) · NOT FOUND.** "pricing…" must be transient — if a thin item shows "pricing…" forever, the thin→"no buyers" branch in `fetchRunePrices` is what fixes it. The Rune Picker auto-polls (~7s, ≤10 tries) to fill "pricing…" hands-free.
- **`/api/trade-status` IP-state numbers are a STALE snapshot** — they only update when a GGG call returns fresh rate-limit headers, so a displayed "7/90" is often old (those calls already aged out). Don't treat it as the live count; the shared `trade-queue.js` self-paces. Still: check it before bursts, and read RATE-LIMITS.md. Local dev shares the **home IP with the user's game client** (prod exits via the gluetun VPN IP), so spaced is fine, bursts hurt their in-game trading.
- **Some currency-exchange items CANNOT be priced from ANY GGG offer endpoint — stop trying.** The Verisium **alloys** (Celestial 160ex, Sovereign 32, Mystic 10, …) and chase orbs: their exalted ask, exalted bid, **divine side**, AND item-search are ALL placeholder noise — 1ex / exactly 1 divine (=319ex this league) / 0.5 divine — decoupled from the real per-item ratio (proven live 2026-06-25, all 3 sides probed). The real ratio exists only in GGG's computed currency-exchange (OAuth cxapi) or poe.ninja. A divine-side fix was tried and **verified wrong** (priced a 9ex item at 160) then reverted. Don't re-attempt offer-data pricing for these. They're served by the **currency-override store** (`.currency-overrides.json` + `CURRENCY_OVERRIDE_SEED`, checked first in `fetchRunePrices`), refreshed via the poe.ninja browser snippet. (Prices are in EXALTED this league; 1 divine ≈ 319 ex, so Celestial 160ex ≈ 0.5 div.)
- **poe.ninja's PoE2 API is Cloudflare-blocked server-side** (404 + `cf-ray`/`server: cloudflare` for EVERY league, even the active one — not a path/league bug; the endpoint `poe.ninja/poe2/api/economy/currencyexchange/overview?leagueName=…&overviewName=Currency` is correct, CF just refuses non-browser clients). So you CANNOT fetch poe.ninja from the server (it'd 404 on the VM too). The only path is a **browser snippet the user runs ON poe.ninja** (CF-cleared, same-origin) → paste back → `POST /api/currency-overrides`. See the Rune Picker `NINJA_SNIPPET`. (This is the one sanctioned poe.ninja use — scoped, on probation; see Data sources + memory `no-poe-ninja-ever`.)
- **Trade2 `/fetch` caps at 10 ids per call** — passing 11+ returns `400 {"error":{"code":2,"message":"Invalid query"}}`. `getTradePrice` correctly slices `result.slice(0,10)`; any ad-hoc probe must too (cost me a confusing debug). The SEARCH returns up to 100 result ids; fetch them in pages of ≤10.
- **Kill stray `node server.js` before verifying.** A zombie server from an earlier throwaway/background run keeps :17777 bound and answers with OLD code, so your fix "doesn't work" / a new endpoint 404s while the file is correct. Check + kill (`Get-CimInstance Win32_Process -Filter "Name='node.exe'" | ? CommandLine -like '*server.js*'`) before spawning a test server.
- **Tablet regex (`buildTablet`): content types OR, desirable mods AND.** A tablet is one mechanic so content `"(breach|ritual)"` = any; but each ticked desirable mod is its OWN quoted block = AND (the tablet must have ALL of them). Was a single `|`-OR group → ticking Effectiveness+Rarity matched pure-Rarity tablets ("shows others" bug, fixed 2026-06-25). **Verify affix TOKENS against GGG `data/stats`** (authoritative mod text) — a throwaway that loads `waystone-data.js` (shim `global.window={}`) and regex-tests each token against the stat list catches false-positives: a bare substring like `men` matched "ELE**men**tal Resistance"/"aug**men**tation" (was Ritual "Omen Chance" `be omen|men` → fixed to `be omen`). Content tokens (`emple`/`verseer`) legitimately match the tablet's TYPE NAME, not a map mod, so they're absent from `data/stats` — that's fine, not dead.
- **Stash regex has NO top-level AND-of-negations, so true combo-keeps can't be expressed.** The dump (`buildDump`) is solo-OR keeps only (keep if rarity≥X OR eff≥40 OR drop≥keep); you cannot do "keep if rarity≥X AND drop≥100 together". Combo valuation lives in the paste **evaluator** (JS: 2+ high rolls → "multi-stat chase, price-check"). Gated buy-side probe (2026-06-25) on corrupted+0-revives T16: Monster Effectiveness ≥40% = real ~10–50ex (KEPT); Monster Rarity (~5ex) and Pack Size (~1ex) are junk solo (NOT kept). Dump's Drop-keep is a typeable selector (default 115, 0=off); `geNum` handles exact 3-digit thresholds.
- **`[hidden]` attribute is defeated by a CSS `display:flex/grid` rule.** Always pair a `display:` rule on a toggled element with `.thing[hidden]{display:none}` (bit the `#bgBar` once).
- **Static assets aren't fingerprinted** — after a deploy, hard-refresh (Ctrl+F5) or the browser serves stale `*.js`/`*.css`. (Plus the mandatory `--build`; see Deploy.)
- **All tool CSS/JS is loaded globally** (linked in `<head>`), so tool CSS must stay prefix-scoped (`.toolroot-<x>`); shared shell bits (e.g. `.bg-bar`) live in index `<style>`.

- 2026-07-01 (latest 118): **Gear Finder BUGFIX — "Require Item Rarity" now catches IMPLICIT rarity (Gold Amulet), not just explicit.** User: amulets showing >20 rarity (unticked) returned 0 when the rarity box was ticked. Root cause (confirmed in data): the floor used `explicit.stat_3917489142` (explicit mods ONLY), but **Gold Amulet's rarity is an IMPLICIT** (`(12-20)% increased Rarity of Items found`) — a different trade id (`implicit.stat_3917489142`); rarity split across two explicit mods also misses a single-mod `min:20`. Trade has no pseudo total-rarity. **Fix:** `injectRarityGroup(q, slot, min)` adds a **`type:"count"` stat-group** (min 1) OR-ing the 4 real rarity sources (explicit/implicit/fractured/rune, each `min:N`) into the final query — replaces the flat preserve floor in BOTH realrank (single-item, the reported path) and optimize-set (buildQ + buildDefenceQ). Deleted the now-dead `rarityFloor`. **The old "count groups 400 on PoE2" note was WRONG — VERIFIED LIVE (2 careful queued calls): a count group WITH a `value` returns 100 results, and a combined and+count query also 200s.** Corrected that gotcha in AGENTS. Local `node -c` clean; smoke **106/0** (offline — no live trade in smoke). **CONFIRMED WORKING on the VM (user, 2026-07-02):** ticking Require Item Rarity ≥20 on amulet now surfaces Gold Amulets (were 0). server.js only → VM auto-deployed.

- 2026-07-01 (latest 116): **Crafter Phase 2b (part 2) — OMENS (Exaltation + Whittling).** Mechanics verified from community (poe.ninja/game8/mobalytics), cited in `craft-engine.js`: **Sinistral=prefix, Dextral=suffix**; **Exaltation** omen forces the next Exalt onto that side; **Whittling** makes Chaos remove the LOWEST-ilvl mod (+add). Two new engine methods in `rankMethods`: (1) **`simulateDirected`** — "directed Exalts": guarantee the hardest target with an essence when available (else Transmute→Regal start), then `directedFill` aims each Exalt at an unmet target's SIDE via `addMod`'s `typeFilter`; cost = start orbs + (Exalt + Exaltation omen)/directed exalt. (2) **`simulateWhittling`** — Alchemy then `removeLowestIlvl`+add chaos loop. Attaches each target's `type` to the normalized `T` (from `byGroup`) for the side logic. Both TESTED (`craft-engine-test.js` **26/26**: whittling removes lowest-ilvl; directed exalt to the suffix always lands a lone suffix target; both methods offered/feasible). **Emergent correctness (validates the models):** for ANY-tier Life+FireRes, directed uses ~½ the exalts (12 vs 22) for equal success, and whittling is WORSE than plain chaos (57% vs 76%) because it can strip a low-tier hit — but for **high-tier** Life-T1+FireRes-T1 whittling is **24.3% vs plain-chaos 2.4% (10×)**, exactly its real use (protect top tiers, churn junk). UI unchanged (methods just appear ranked; 6 rows render clean, no overflow, 0 console errors). ~4.2s worst-case sim (6 methods, 2 chaos loops); smoke **105/0**. **NEXT: Phase 2c desecration** (Well of Souls / bone mechanic — the `soul`/abyss-gated mods excluded from the normal pool; most research-heavy) → **Phase 3 price-weighting** (rank by Divine via poe.ninja proxy — will reshuffle essence/exalt/omen-heavy routes vs cheap alchemy/chaos; ranking is by ORB COUNT today, caveat shown in UI).
- 2026-07-01 (latest 115): **Crafter Phase 2b (part 1) — ESSENCE crafting method.** Essences guarantee ONE specific mod for the item's class (only one essence per item; mechanics from maxroll/community, cited in `craft-engine.js`). `simulateEssence` (engine): among the targets, guarantees the essence-available one that's HARDEST to hit randomly (lowest summed accepted-tier weight = biggest payoff), then MC-fills 5 exalts and checks all targets; cost = 1 Essence + fill Exalts. **Key correctness guard:** an essence only applies if its forced mod key is a tier you ACCEPTED — otherwise it occupies the group slot and would BLOCK your wanted tier (tested). Added to `rankMethods` via `opts.essences`. **Server:** `craftEssenceOptions(base,ilvl)` builds the class's essence→mod options from `CRAFT_DATA.essences`, skipping essence-exclusive mods not in ModItem (Perfect/EssenceDisplay*) and tiers above ilvl; passed into the simulate call. - 2026-07-01 (latest 107): **FIX landed — the bow now surfaces (Blood Volley = ★best value +15,125); fixed a ranked-vs-paste scoring gap (dropped quality).** User confirmed the latest-105/106 filter works. They noticed the ranked score (+15,125) ≠ the paste/Evaluate score (+32,308) for the SAME bow. Two causes: (1) **rune normalization** — `pobItemFromTradeEntry` deliberately strips the candidate's runes and fills its sockets with YOUR current rune (apples-to-apples: a rune is fungible, socketable into any bow, so a bow shouldn't be credited for its listed rune); paste keeps the item's own runes → higher. This is intended (explained to user, offered to change). (2) **dropped quality** — the reconstruction omitted the item's `Quality: +N%`, so PoB scored fetched items at 0% quality (materially low for local weapon/armour values). FIXED: `pobItemFromTradeEntry` now reads `item.properties` Quality and emits a `Quality: +N%` line. Improves accuracy for ALL fetched weapons/armour, not just this bow. smoke 68/0. server.js only → VM auto-deploys. (Open question posed to user: should the ranked score keep the BOW'S OWN runes instead of normalizing to yours, to match the paste/real value? Deferred to their preference.)

So each top-2 weighted-stat pool now floors at `Math.max(1, round(w.cur))` where `w.cur` = your current roll of that stat (already in `weights` from /api/gear/weights, passed through realrank). - 2026-07-01 (latest 102): **Verified live why the Blood Volley bow still wasn't found — corrected wrong theories + removed dead code.** User insisted the bow IS instant-buyable (found it in-game) — they were right. Ran 3 careful throwaway Trade2 probes (queue, spaced, deleted): (a) **the bow IS in the securable pool** — 10,000+ securable bows with +4 proj levels ≤900 div exist; my "not in securable pool" theory was WRONG. (b) **Sort-key truth:** only `price` + `dps` are valid sort keys on a bow search; **`pdps`/`edps` 400 "Invalid query"**, and `statgroup.0` 400s unless a `type:weight` group is present. So latest-101's `pdps` sub-pool was DEAD (400'd every call, swallowed by try/catch, wasted a rate-limited search) — removed it; kept the working `dps` sub-pool + the proj-levels weight. (c) **The real reason it's missed:** the bow's raw weapon `dps` is mid-pack among 10k, and its linear weighted-stat sum is mid-pack too, so it sits outside BOTH the weighted top-100 and the `dps` top-30 — yet PoB scores it +88,913. Fundamental linear-sort-vs-real-DPS limit over a huge pool; no cheap sort reliably catches it. Paste-to-score is the per-item answer (memory [[trade2-weapon-sort-keys]]). Next lever (NOT shipped, needs VM verify): a sub-pool that REQUIRES the build's #1 weighted stat (proj-levels) then ranks by `dps`, to shrink 10k→the bows that carry the key stat — but proj-filter + `dps`-sort returned 400 in one probe (possibly the same-query soft-400 artifact, unconfirmed). smoke 68/0. server.js only → VM auto-deploys.

- 2026-06-30 (latest 91): **Gear Finder shows READABLE fetch errors instead of raw browser exceptions.** User hit "Failed: TypeError: NetworkError when attempting to fetch resource" (a fetch that landed during the VM's redeploy downtime — confirmed the VM was back up, HTTP 200). Crucially it still parses JSON FIRST so our endpoints' real `{error}` messages (returned even on 4xx, e.g. "Pick 2-5 slots", rate-limited) pass through unchanged — only infra failures get translated. - 2026-07-03 (latest 95): **Craft Advisor Phase-2a: Annul/Exalt "reroll a jammed side" route + honest AMORTIZED costing.** Follow-up to latest-94 (the user asked to push success rates up). **(1)** New engine variant `simulateFinishAnnul` (`craft-engine.js`, wired into `rankFinish`): when a target's side jams with junk, directed-Annul (Sinistral/Dextral Annulment omen) unjams it, then re-Exalt — repeated tries on the SAME item. Crucially its target set `Tall` includes the KEPT groups (annul removes a RANDOM mod on the side → can destroy a kept mod = failure), so the risk is modeled. Lifts one-shot success a lot (verified on the real ring: add Life 25%→**65%**, add Life+Cold 5%→**28%**). **(2)** BUT modeling it exposed a costing bug — with a directed OMEN on every op, its raw per-attempt cost balloons (~145 div at 28% for a cheap ring — a trap). Fix: **cost is now AMORTIZED** (`expectedOrbs ÷ p` in both `simulateFinish` + `simulateFinishAnnul`) = expected orbs to END UP WITH the item, retrying cheap magic/rare bases when an attempt bricks. That's the number that compares to resale, and it self-corrects: for the ring the ★ is "spam bases, **2.66 div** expected" while the Annul route (518 div amortized) is correctly dominated — surfaced only as a collapsible **"More reliable on this item: X div · Y% per attempt"** for when you can't rebase a specific item. `successPerAttempt` stays the one-shot % (per-item brick risk shown in the recipe). **(3)** Advisor ranks candidates by ACHIEVABILITY: deepest finish whose amortized cost stays under a cap (`FINISH_DIV_CAP=15` div / `FINISH_ORB_CAP=400`) is ★; pricier over-crafts (3-mod ring = 4155 div) sink, dimmed "— a stretch". `best` = cheapest-amortized non-brick-prone method; `reliable` = a notably-higher one-shot alt (the Annul route). Verified end-to-end (headless Playwright, 0 console errors): ★ Add Life+Cold 2.66 div, safer Add Life 0.28 div, dimmed 3-mod stretch. Tests: craft-engine +2 (52, annul beats pure-exalt on a jammed side + spends annuls & exalts), smoke 106/0. ponytail: the div cap is a flat heuristic (tune per feedback). server.js + client → VM auto-deploys.
- 2026-07-02 (latest 94): **Crafter: "Craft Advisor" — paste an item, get the best finish route (no manual target picking).** User wanted to drop an item (e.g. a Magic ring with T1 res + phys) and be told what to add to make it valuable + the exact steps, since they don't know the meta combos/techniques. Design: hybrid — suggest target + route + craft COST instantly (offline, free), price RESALE value on demand (a button, budgeted Trade2). Optimizes for resale ("what sells"). **New engine path** (`craft-engine.js`): `seedItem`/`simulateFinish`/`rankFinish` — SEEDS the sim with the pasted item's current mods (kept, self-satisfying) then Regal (if Magic) + directed Exalts toward the FILL targets; it's `simulateDirected` with a pre-seed, no new mechanics. **Cost is per-attempt, NOT amortized by 1/p** (you have one item — a miss bricks it; Annul-recovery is Phase 2), and `successPerAttempt` is the honest one-shot chance. Cap budget subtracts kept mods from the 3/3. **Mapping** (`server.js`): mod TEXT → craft-data group via `buildCraftGroupIndex` (pool-scoped + single-stat + type-checked — this AVOIDS the mis-maps a global text match makes: "+X to maximum Life" → a suffix unique-mutation, "Rarity" → a fishing mod; pool-scoping to `craftModList` kills both). Desirable aliases → group via `ALIAS_TEMPLATE` (exact normalized templates) + `ALIAS_EXPAND` (composites like totalElementalRes→3 res). `generateCraftCandidates` keeps mapped current mods, fills open slots from `UPGRADE_SEARCH_STATS[slot]`, makes 1–3 depth variants; `craftRecipeSteps` renders the ordered recipe (Sinistral=prefix / Dextral=suffix Exaltation omens). **Endpoints**: `POST /api/craft/advise` (offline: paste → ranked candidates, deepest-practical-first) and `POST /api/craft/resale` (on-demand: mirrors `/api/gear/basic-link`, gated on `tradeStatus()`, 1 search + 1 fetch → cheapest-cluster div; caller passes `category` from `gearSlotCfg`, NOT the bare slot — "ring" 400s, "accessory.ring" works). **UI** (`index.html`/`craft.js`/`craft.css`): "✦ Suggest the best craft" button appears on paste of a Magic/Rare item → `renderAdvise` shows candidates (chips + numbered steps + cost/odds) with a "Check resale value" button per candidate → profit = resale − cost. **Verified end-to-end via headless Playwright + live HTTP**: ring paste → keeps fire-res+phys, ★ "add Life+Cold (0.16 div, 5% one-shot)" + safer "add Life (0.08 div, 24%)" + dimmed impractical 3-mod; 0 console errors; live `/api/craft/resale` returned a real cheapest-div floor + count + trade URL. Tests: craft-engine +4 (50, seeded-finish beats from-scratch + per-attempt Regal=1 + over-cap), smoke 106/0. **Phase 2 (deferred, flagged):** reroll junk current mods (Annul/Chaos), weapon hybrid mapping, tier-based resale mins (v1 uses min:1 → rough floor), over-cap "make room" advice, desecration. server.js + client → VM auto-deploys.
- 2026-07-02 (latest 93): **Crafter now uses REAL spawn weights (Craft of Exile) — was treating every mod tier as equally likely.** Follow-up to latest-92's weight finding. Confirmed the root cause on the VM's own PoB data: `ModItem.lua` `weightVal` is a binary 1/0 eligibility gate (grep: only 0s and 1s exist), no other PoB Data file carries weights, and PoE2 spawn weights were **never in the game client** — GGG didn't ship them; Craft of Exile derived them (recombinator experiments + trade parsing). So our extraction was faithful; the data just wasn't there, making top-tier crafts look far too easy. Fix pipeline: **(1)** `gen-craft-weights.js` (new) fetches CoE's `https://www.craftofexile.com/json/poe2/main/poec_data.json` (a `poecd={…}` JS assignment; strip the prefix) and overlays real per-tier, per-base-archetype `weighting` onto each mod as `mod.cw = {archetype: weight}`, rewriting craft-data.js. **JOIN** (worked out live via the CoE data globals in-browser): CoE `modifier.name_modifier` is a `#`-templated stat line → normalize PoB stat text the same way (roll ranges/bare numbers→`#`, strip commas — CoE joins hybrid lines with ", ") and match on (template + affix), then tier by exact ilvl, then base by archetype. CoE's modgroup NAMES are unreliable (drops "Local" inconsistently: `LocalFireDamage`→`FireDamage` but keeps `LocalPhysicalDamagePercent`), so stat-text is the join key, not group. **(2)** `craft-archetype.js` (new, shared) maps a PoB base (class+tags) → CoE base archetype name: weapons/jewellery by class name; armour by attribute tag (`str_armour`→"(STR)", `str_dex_armour`→"(STR/DEX)", …, no CoE triple so str_dex_int→binary fallback); wand/staff element = the one spell type NOT excluded by a `no_<elem>_spell_mods` tag (cold→"Ice"). **(3)** server.js `craftEffWeight(mod, tagset, archKey)`: PoB binary weight still decides ELIGIBILITY (authoritative — a mod PoB says can't roll is excluded), but eligible mods use `mod.cw[archKey]` when present, else binary fallback (1) → no regression. `craftPool`/`craftModList` resolve the archetype once per base. **Coverage 94.5%** of eligible (base×mod) slots get a real weight; unmatched (a few order-swapped hybrid mods, generic casters, Charm/Jewel/Flask whose pools live in other PoB files) keep binary. **Verified end-to-end via live HTTP**: Warmonger Bow ilvl80, phys% top tier (iL75) is now weight **50** vs **1000** base tier (20× rarer — was 1:1); the user's "0.02% chaos spam" complaint is now correctly modeled (`/api/craft/simulate` returns chaos_spam at **0.08%/att, flagged impractical & sunk**, ★ = the realistic Erasure route), where the old equal-weight model wrongly showed chaos spam at ~5%. craft-data.js barely grew (1.17→1.18MB, compact JSON). Tests: craft-data-test +3 (18, asserts top tier rarer than base + binary preserved), craft-engine 46, smoke 106/0. **Re-bake on league/data update:** `luajit gen-craft-data.lua && node gen-craft-weights.js` (Lua footer now prints this reminder). Runtime stays offline — weights are baked. server.js + craft-data.js → VM auto-deploys.
- 2026-07-02 (latest 92): **Crafter: "impractical" routes (raw chaos spam etc.) are flagged, sunk below realistic routes, and never recommended.** User (bow craft: T1 phys + crit) reported the tool "recommends alchemy + chaos spam with 0.02% success and 120 chaos assumed" — unrealistic. Root cause: `rankMethods` costed EVERY route as `perAttemptCost / p` and ranked purely by that expected total, so a route that completes on <2% of fresh bases (you'd reroll the WHOLE item 50+ times, scrapping currency each miss) was still presented as a costed plan — its `expectedOrbs` is a `cap/p` extrapolation nobody runs. Fix (craft-engine.js): new `PRACTICAL_MIN = 0.02`; each feasible method gets `impractical = successPerAttempt < PRACTICAL_MIN`, and the sort is `(impractical) || totalOrbs` so impractical routes always fall below realistic ones. server.js `priceCraftMethods` sort mirrors it (impractical last even if their theoretical divine cost looks cheap — cheap chaos × 0.02% is a fantasy number). Client (craft.js/craft.css): the ★ now marks the first NON-impractical feasible route (not just index 0); impractical rows are dimmed, headline cost reads "impractical", and the sub reads "only X%/attempt — you'd reroll the whole item ~N× (theoretical …). Not a real route; use a targeted method above." When EVERY route is impractical, a banner says the combo is too rare and to loosen a tier / use essence+omens. Verified against the real Warmonger Bow ilvl80 pool: for T1 phys + T5 crit the ★ shifts from a reroll route to Erasure-omen (60%/att); the 0.02–0.9% reroll routes get flagged + sunk. craft-engine-test +5 checks (46 total), craft-data-test 15, smoke 106/0. **SEPARATE DEEPER ISSUE FOUND, NOT FIXED (needs its own pass):** every mod spawn weight in craft-data.js is 0 or 1 (confirmed: 3322 mods weight 1, 1224 weight 0 — no other values), so the sim treats every tier as EQUALLY likely. Real PoE2 weights range into the hundreds/thousands and make high tiers much rarer, so ALL crafter odds are off (optimistic for top tiers). `gen-craft-data.lua` reads `m.weightVal[i]` — either PoB-PoE2 stores real weights elsewhere or the field isn't populated; needs investigating the PoB Data format. Flagged for the user.

- 2026-06-30 (latest 85): **Set Optimizer: REMOVED the per-slot resistance preserve floors — they were excluding the exact rebalance items the optimizer exists to find.** User: single-slot found 2 great upgrades "that would go together," but the 2-slot set "only found DPS losses" (i.e. it evaluated other combos, never those two). Root cause: the set's per-slot pool query added a hard `and`-gate requiring each replacement to keep ≥70% of EVERY resistance the current item provides (added latest-75 to stop a swap dropping a breakpoint). That makes the set pools NARROWER than single-slot (which has no such floor) and structurally forbids break-here/recover-there: a chest with 0 chaos res can't enter the chest pool even if a ring would recover the chaos. So the items single-slot surfaces are excluded from the set, and only res-preserving (worse) combos get scored. Fix: deleted the per-slot res-floor loop; per-slot pools are now the SAME breadth as single-slot (defence-sorted, ungated, rarity floor still honored). Resistance correctness is enforced by the EXISTING combined guards — the additive pre-screen (sums each changed slot's breakpoint DELTA, so a drop on one slot + recover on another nets out) and `checkBreakpoints` on the real `calcMulti` (every shown set provably holds all breakpoints). So the optimizer can now actually do its job: find the complementary pair. Trade-off (acceptable, intended UX): with broad pools, more combos are illegal → if NONE hold the breakpoints you'll see "no legal set / all held-but-downgrade" sooner → dial a breakpoint down to probe. `curStats` decl removed (was only used by the deleted block). smoke 103/0. server.js only → VM auto-deploys.
- 2026-06-30 (latest 84): **Set Optimizer ("group") pools go deeper — 10 → 30 candidates/slot (2-3 slots), and the fetch is chunked.** User: single-slot "seems to be working better" (latest-83 fix landed; the exact deflection chest still didn't surface but user is OK with that — it's the raw-evasion-rank/deflection-invisible-to-sort limit), but "group one [Set Optimizer] doesn't work that good, go deeper into the search." - 2026-06-30 (latest 83): **THE actual exclusion bug: defence slots were HARD-GATED on the top stats, excluding single-axis EHP items.** User retested chest: status showed "ranked by defence — highest-EHP first" + 100 scored (so latest-80/81/82 all landed — the `ev` sort key IS valid, depth works) but the +556 EHP chest was STILL missing. The defence sort + deep PoB scoring (top 100 single-slot) ranks the real winner without pre-filtering on stats the item happens to lack. On a defence-sort 400 it falls back to the full `buildQ(false)`. smoke 103/0. server.js only → VM auto-deploys. **Retest chest:** the Blood Suit-class chests should now appear (they're no longer gated out). Honest, but confusing — could add a tiny weighted probe to verify the cookie if it bugs the user.
- 2026-06-30 (latest 82): **Single-slot realrank now PoB-scores the whole search page (100), not 50 — stop trusting the heuristic sort to pre-pick winners.** User's point: "the whole point of this tool is not to manual scan." Right — paste-to-score is a per-item check, not the product. - 2026-06-30 (latest 81): **FOLLOWUP to 80: the defence sort was being UNDONE by the candidate-pick logic.** After latest-80 the user retested chest and the +556 EHP chest was STILL missing; the status line read "price spread." Root cause: realrank's pick step is `const pick = weighted ? all.slice(0,m) : <spread sample across the whole result page>` — for defence slots I'd forced `weighted=false`, so even though the SEARCH was sorted by defence desc, the pick SAMPLED A SPREAD across it instead of taking the top-m highest-defence. So the sort did nothing. Fix: (1) `pick = (weighted || usedDefenceSort) ? all.slice(0,m) : spread` — defence-sorted pools take the top-m like weighted; (2) track `usedDefenceSort` (cleared if the defence-sort 400s and reverts), return it as `sortMode` ("defence"/"weighted"/"price"); (3) client status line now shows **"(ranked by defence — highest-EHP first)"** when the defence sort actually ran, so the next live test is self-diagnosing (if it still says "price spread", the `ev`/`ar`/`es` sort key 400'd and self-disabled → key name is wrong, try long form). **Still NEEDS the same VM live verify** (latest-80's key question is unresolved until a real run shows the sortMode). **Expectation caveat told to user:** even a working defence sort may not surface THIS exact chest — its EHP comes largely from "Gain Deflection = 20% of Evasion" + 3 rune sockets, so it can be mid-pack on RAW evasion while top on real EHP; no linear trade sort captures that, only PoB scoring does. - 2026-06-29 (latest 71): **CORRECTION + real fix: the latest-70 rune-socket valuation added ZERO — caught by testing it on the user's `Main.xml`.** User said "i saved a build called main test it." Ran the real PoB (local, `Main.xml`, no trade calls): duplicating the `{rune}` mod line per socket changed EHP/DPS by **0**. Root cause: PoB serializes runes tagged `{enchant}{rune}` and **combines identical runes into one summed line** (the user's chest = 2× Perfect Iron Rune → a single `40% increased AES`), and the **`{enchant}` tag makes PoB treat the value as a fixed enchant that does NOT stack on duplication** (nor on numeric edit). Verified the fix empirically on a clean Corsair Coat: **PLAIN (untagged) mod text DOES stack** — `20% AES ×2` == `40% AES ×1`, `+40 Life ×2` == `+80 Life ×1`. **Real model:** `extractRuneFill(currentRaw)` now returns `{lines, sockets}` — the rune mod lines stripped of ALL `{..}` markup + the `Bonded:` prefix (→ plain stackable text), and `sockets` = your filled rune-socket count (`Rune:` lines). `pobItemFromTradeEntry(entry, extraImplicits, runeFill)` DROPS the seller's runeMods and emits YOUR rune block scaled by `candidateSockets / yourSockets` (each number ×factor), so an extra socket adds rune value and an unsocketable base loses it. **Live-proven on Main.xml:** chest EHP across 0/1/2/3 sockets = 21190 / 22154 / 23413 / 24736 (extra socket ≈ +1.3k EHP); helmet 23846→27235; gloves/boots Δ0 on EHP (their runes are attack/movement speed — correct, value shows in DPS not EHP). `test-socket-fill.js` rewritten for the scaling model (2sk→×1, 3sk→×1.5=60%, 1sk→×0.5=20%, 0sk→none, seller rune dropped, legacy path intact) — **green**, `node --check` clean. **ponytail:** scaling assumes a uniform rune across your sockets (exact for same-rune-in-every-socket, the common case + the user's; a mix of different runes scales proportionally, not exactly); still drops niche base "Bonded" mods. Renamed export `extractRuneLines`→`extractRuneFill`. **Supersedes latest-70's "it works" claim.** VM auto-deploys on push (no PoB-bridge change).
- 2026-06-29 (latest 70): **Gear Finder now values RUNE SOCKETS — an extra/empty socket counts as room for one more of YOUR rune (exceptional bases were being ignored).** User asked whether the optimizer values extra sockets ("exceptional gear"); it did not. The candidate text grafted the SELLER's `runeMods` as implicits (`pobItemFromTradeEntry`), so empty sockets scored 0 and a 2-socket base read no better than a 1-socket one. **Probed the live trade2 JSON (1 search + 1 fetch, through the queue): `item.sockets` is a per-socket array (`[{group,type:"rune"},…]`) → `sockets.length` = total sockets incl. empty; `socketedItems[].socket` indexes into it (standard GGG all-sockets schema); seller `runeMods` mix the rune effect + base "Bonded" lines and are per-rune.** Fix: new `extractRuneLines(currentRaw)` pulls YOUR per-socket rune (PoB tags rune mods `{rune}`); `pobItemFromTradeEntry(entry, extraImplicits, runeLines)` now DROPS the seller's runeMods and fills EVERY socket with your rune (`sockets.length ×`), so an extra socket = +1 of your rune, a no-socket base loses it entirely. Flows into both DPS (`pob.calc` on the text) and breakpoint contrib (`parseItemStats` on the same text) automatically. Wired into the two upgrade-finders: optimize-set (per-slot `currentRaw`) + single-slot realrank (`input.current.raw`); the cheapest-at-DPS check (`/api/gear/cheaper`) left on legacy (no clean per-slot current there). Exported both fns + `test-socket-fill.js` (pure string logic: 2 sockets→rune×2, seller rune dropped, base explicit kept, 0 sockets→×0, legacy path unchanged) — **green**. **ponytail:** drops base "Bonded" mods (niche Shaman/expedition bases only) — add back if they matter. **NOT live-verified end-to-end** (no build XML present locally; the one residual assumption — PoB summing N identical `{rune}` implicit lines — is the existing proven runeMods-as-implicits path, but eyeball one real run: multi-socket bases should now jump in ΔDPS/ΔEHP). - 2026-06-28 (latest 67): **NEW — Passive Tree move planner (🌳 in Gear Finder). Pure PoB, no Trade2.** "Which points to move for DPS." Feasibility probe (temp `--treepower`/`--treemoves`, now a clean command): PoB's misc calculator supports `addNodes`/`removeNodes` overrides (it's how PoB colors its own tree — `PassiveTreeView.lua:1889`), and after `spec:BuildAllDependsAndPaths()` every node has `pathDist` (points-to-reach), `node.path` (route), `node.depends` (what breaks if removed). So: for each unallocated Notable within `maxDepth`, `calcFunc({addNodes=node.path})` → DPS/EHP gained; for each allocated Notable, `calcFunc({removeNodes=node.depends})` → DPS/EHP lost (and `#depends` = points freed). - 2026-06-27 (latest 41): **Gear Finder upgrade search — generic fix for base-defensive slots (equipment-total filter + floor only on stats the item has).** User: the chest fix can't be tuned to their build, it must work for ANY build (it's becoming a full suite). Root cause (diagnosed live): the realrank stat-floors only used the top-2 MARGINAL-weighted stats, which for an evasion chest are cold/chaos res (high marginal value under-cap), NOT the chest's ~2800 evasion (saturated → tiny marginal weight) — and a cur=0 "would-help" stat got forced to a `≥1` floor, excluding the item's own type. So the search returned res chests that drop evasion and tank EHP. **Fix (build-agnostic):** (1) `computeGearWeights` now parses the item's TOTAL base defences from its property lines (`Evasion:`/`Armour:`/`Energy Shield:` → `equip:{ev,ar,es}`) — note PoB writes `Evasion:` not `Evasion Rating:`, which the stat-parser's evasion regex missed. (2) realrank adds `equipment_filters` (`ev`/`ar`/`es`/`dps`, floored 70%) so a replacement KEEPS the item's core total defence. (3) floors now only use stats the item actually HAS (`cur>0`) — what it IS, not what it could gain. Verified live in the QUICK scan (scoreCap-10): chest **Damnation Veil +4428 EHP @350div** (was nothing), boots **Agony Urge +604 EHP @0.26div** (hybrid ev+es auto-parsed), bow +28k (no defensive total → equip `{}`, still works). smoke 114/0. CAVEAT: amulet/ring DPS slots have no equipment-total to constrain the pool, so a deep upgrade can still fall outside the scan's top-10 (the cur>0 broadening can push it out) — the drill-in "Rank by real DPS" (scoreCap-50) finds it; that's the known scan-depth limit, not a regression in the fix.

- 2026-06-27 (latest 39): **POESESSID was never loaded locally — added a zero-dep `.env` loader.** User: "didn't I give you a POESESSID to tackle this?" — and they're right it wasn't working. Root cause: `server.js` read `process.env.POESESSID` but **nothing loaded `.env`** for a local `node server.js` run (only Docker passed it via compose `POESESSID=${POESESSID:-}` from the host `.env` next to docker-compose.yml). Fix = exclude the want's side from `have`, exactly like EE2 (Divine→[exalted,chaos], Chaos→[divine,exalted]). **Verified live: divine 350ex (exalted-side), chaos 43.75ex (divine-side 0.125div×350).** Per user's call: Rune Picker now (1) shows all 3 currency sides per row like EE2 (`sideLine` e.g. "2 ex · 1 div · 0.1 c" in native units — read the right denomination yourself); (2) passes the pasted **qty as `minimum`** (EE2's stack filter — drops 1-item par-spam; verified it changes the book). **Dropped from the Rune Picker** (EE2 has none of them): bid-first pricing, ≥2ex gate, "no buyers/thin", cluster/bait filters, item-search fallback, the curated/poe.ninja override. - 2026-06-26 (latest 27): **Currency pricing now uses Exiled-Exchange's exact method — the "unpriceable" alloys price LIVE off GGG (poe.ninja/override no longer primary).** Root cause of the user's "5000% off": (a) the alloys were served from a STALE baked override (`Celestial Alloy: 160`), and (b) where we did read the exchange we queried `have: exalted` ONLY + ran spam filters that mangle the book. **Read Exiled-Exchange-2's source (Kvan7/Exiled-Exchange-2, `pathofexile-bulk.ts`):** its currency algo = ONE bulk-exchange call `have:[divine,exalted,chaos] want:[id]`, single-offer listings, sort by ratio (`exchange÷item`), drop sub-½ bait, take cheapest cluster per side. Ported as **`exchangePriceEx(league, id, divineEx, chaosEx)`** + `sideCheapestRatio` (server.js, near `fetchExchangeData`): multi-have read, prefer the EXALTED side (base unit / real market for sub-divine items), fall back to divine/chaos × rate. Per-item exchange calls are slower than the old batched read but correct; single-user so fine. (Exiled itself is per-user client-side w/ its own IP + 5-min cache + debounce — we're server-side but single-user, so pacing is a non-issue.)

- 2026-06-26 (latest 25): **Gear Finder: melee/2H weapons now import (base→class map from PoB's own GGG data), + per-base implicits.** Fixes the latent gap where `pobWeaponSlot` keyword-matched the base name → sword/axe/mace/dagger/claw/flail bases whose name lacks the class word (e.g. "Gladius", "Felled Greatclub") returned null → the weapon was silently DROPPED from the import. **`gen-pob-bases.js`** parses PoB's `Data/Bases/*.lua` (auto-generated, "(c) GGG" — the authoritative local equivalent of poedb's all-bases list, no scraping) → emits **`pob-bases.js`** = `{ baseName: { slot, implicit? } }` (1735 bases). `pobWeaponSlot` now matches the item's base-type line against this map FIRST (handles quarterstaves too — PoB types them `Staff`/subType `Warstaff` → mapped to `quarterstaff`, not caster `staff`), keyword sniff only as fallback for magic items (base buried in name). `reconstructItem` (baseless paste) grafts the base's real implicit at mid-roll for a truer score. `server.js` requires `pob-bases.js` (guarded — missing file just falls back to keywords). Verified all 15 weapon classes resolve from real base names; smoke 119/0. **Re-run `node gen-pob-bases.js` on the Main PC after a league/PoB data update.** (Magic weapons with the base embedded in a prefixed name still rely on the keyword fallback — rare in real builds.)
- 2026-06-26 (latest 24): **Gear Finder: +skills now WEIGHTED + SEARCHED (heuristic gap closed).** Root cause: the existing skill-level keys (`levelAllSpellSkills`/`levelAllMinionSkills`/`projectileLevels`) were in the filter lists but had **no `GEAR_PROBE_TEMPLATES` entry**, so `computeGearWeights` never perturbed them → 0 weight → never sent as search mods. Slot lists: martial set (`bow`, shared by all martial weapons) gets attack+melee; `amulet` gets attack. **Scope kept tight per user:** skipped element-specific spell-skill levels (`levelAllSpellSkills` already values any spell build) and anything from the `enchant` group (anointments) — only normal explicit rolls. Verified: GGG ids correct, PoB's mod DB recognizes all five exact texts (`grep Data/`), parser reads them. NOT measured live as a DPS *number* — Ammyproper.xml has TotalDPS 0 (no active skill gem), so a skill-level perturbation can't move DPS on it; will weight correctly on any build with an active skill. **STILL not added (real PoB score already counts them via full item text):** generic `+to Level of all Skills`/element skills — left out as uncertain-provenance/niche.
- 2026-06-26 (latest 23): **Gear Finder: "Score together" — real combined gain for all pins (one PoB calc), not the approximate sum.** New bridge command **`CALCM`** (`pob-bridge.lua` `calcMulti`) equips SEVERAL items at once (one per slot) via PoB's own `new("Item", …)` parser + `itemsTab:AddItem`/`slot.selItemId`, recomputes, reads stats, then **restores** (reverts selItemId + DeleteItem) so the persistent process stays clean. - 2026-06-26 (latest 22): **+skills ARE scored by the real PoB number, but NOT by the search/weight heuristic.** Headless scoring (paste-an-item, realrank, the new combined "Score together") feeds full item text to PoB, so `+to Level of all Spell/Minion/Projectile Skills` etc. already move ΔDPS correctly. - 2026-06-26 (latest 15): **Gear Finder value-check is now PoB-based, not stat-thresholds.** The old "price floor" matched 2-3 stat thresholds → useless ("top rolls from 0 div, 6739 listed" — 1000s of junk clear a couple thresholds). User's instinct was right: only PoB tells you an item is actually as good. Rewrote `POST /api/gear/value-check`: searches instant-buyout items of the slot **priced UNDER** this candidate (gated on its top-2 rolls for relevance), cheapest-first, **scores each in PoB** (loads buildXml, swaps into pobSlot), returns the cheapest whose ΔDPS ≥ 90% of this item's — i.e. "same DPS for less" (you'd overpay) or "best price — none of N cheaper match". Button "best price?" shows only for upgrades costing ≥1 div. Scores ≤20 (2 fetch calls) per click. - 2026-06-26 (latest 14): **Gear Finder value tools: free ★ best-value tag + on-demand "price floor" check.** (1) ★ best-value: ranks the scored candidates by gain-per-exalted (DPS, else EHP) and tags the best — FREE, from data we already have. (2) `POST /api/gear/value-check` (1 search + 1 fetch on a per-row "price floor" button): searches instant-buyout items of the slot with AT LEAST the item's top-3 weighted rolls, sorted price asc, returns count + cheapest price. **Honest framing matters here:** trade filters on individual stats, not overall power, and a DPS build's weighted stats don't include its life/res — so even at the item's real rolls there are thousands of matches (verified: AS16+phys18 → 3551 items, cheapest 1ex). So the verdict is the FLOOR price for the item's *key rolls* ("top rolls start at X — you're paying extra for the other mods"), NOT "identical item, cheaper exists" (that would mislead). `gearStatFilters(mods, limit)` now takes a cap (realrank still 2, value-check 3). The accurate "best deal" signal remains the ★ (real PoB DPS/ex). smoke 79/0.

- 2026-06-26 (latest 6): **Gear Finder realrank scored EVERY candidate identically — `pobItemFromTradeEntry` fed PoB "object Object" mod lines.** PoE2 trade2 returns each mod as an OBJECT (`{description, hash, mods:[...]}`), NOT a plain string like PoE1. The old `.map(normalizePoeMarkup)` did `String(obj)` → `"[object Object]"` → PoB parsed a valid base with NO mods → every fetched item = a blank glove → identical ΔDPS/ΔEHP (the user's "-47,138 DPS" on all 10). - 2026-06-26 (latest 5): **REAL root cause of the gear-finder "Invalid query" 400 — Trade2 /fetch caps at 10 ids (realrank sent 12).** Proven LIVE (via the VM's own endpoints over Tailscale, `http://REDACTED-TAILNET-IP-A:17777`, exact gluetun egress): the SEARCH was always fine — realrank with a 0-result query returns cleanly; `basic-link` (search only) 200s; realrank (search **+ fetch**) 400s. Direct test: `/api/trade2/fetch` with **11 ids → HTTP 400 "Invalid query"**, **10 ids → 200**. realrank did `slice(0, 12)`; the **70% stat floor widened results past 10**, exposing a latent bug (readOneBand already chunks by 10). Fix = `slice(0, 10)` (we only score ≤10 anyway) + the fetch is now wrapped so its errors are labelled by stage instead of logging the *search* query (that misleading error sent me chasing league/pseudo/IP theories for hours — **all of those earlier diagnoses below were WRONG; the league/pseudo/empty-group fixes are harmless improvements but were NOT the bug**). Verify after redeploy: realrank on a slot with >10 in-budget candidates should now score them. Diagnostic trick worth keeping: the VM app is reachable over Tailscale, so you can drive its exact egress with `curl http://REDACTED-TAILNET-IP-A:17777/api/gear/{basic-link,realrank}` without SSH.
- 2026-06-26 (latest 4): **Gear Finder "Invalid query" 400 — ROOT CAUSE = wrong LEAGUE in the search URL (not the body).** After surfacing the failing query (gloves, attackSpeed + flatPhysAttack, price div≤250) I reproduced it LIVE: the **identical body returns 200 on a good league and `{code:2,"Invalid query"}` on a bad league** — both individual stat ids and the 2-stat combo are valid. The league lives in `/api/trade2/search/poe2/{league}`, NOT the query body (which is what the debug logged), so a stale/wrong client `state.league` poisons every gear search even though other tools (which use a good league) work from the same NordVPN IP. Fix: new `gearTradeSearch(q, league)` helper — POSTs the search and, on a 400 with a non-default league, **retries once on `DEFAULT_LEAGUE`** ("Runes of Aldur"); both realrank + basic-link use it (basic-link returns the league actually used in its trade URL). The realrank 400 error now also prints `league=…`. NOTE: gear-finder is the only tool that trusted a client-supplied league; the self-heal aligns it with the others. `node --check` + smoke **79/0**. If a user still 400s, the surfaced `league=` reveals the bad value (and a browser hard-refresh rules out cached old JS — `gear-finder.js` is NOT cache-busted in index.html).
- 2026-06-26 (latest 3): **Gear Finder realrank/basic-link "Invalid query" (HTTP 400) fix.** After the 70%-floor change a real query reached Trade2 and 400'd (`code 2, Invalid query`). Cause: both `/api/gear/realrank` and `/api/gear/basic-link` filtered stat ids to `^explicit\.stat_\d+$` only — but ES/life map to **pseudo** ids (`pseudo.pseudo_total_energy_shield`, `pseudo.pseudo_total_life`), so on an ES/life slot every top stat was stripped, leaving `stats: [{type:"and",filters:[]}]` — and PoE2 trade rejects an empty `and` group. Fix: new shared helpers `gearStatFilters()` (keeps explicit **and** pseudo ids, top 2, floored) + `gearStatGroup()` (omits the stats group entirely when empty), used by both endpoints. Verified: regex keeps explicit+pseudo / drops equipment-filter ids (`dps`/`ev`), empty→`[]`, `node --check` clean, smoke **79/0** (browser skipped). **LIVE-VERIFIED (3 spaced queue calls from the Main PC, no limit trip):** the realrank query shape returns 200; `pseudo.pseudo_total_energy_shield` is a VALID PoE2 stat id (321 hits); the fixed ES-chest path (pseudo ES + explicit life, 2-stat `and` + budget) returns 200. So the bug was real and the fix is correct. **If the user STILL gets the identical 400 after this, it's stale code on the VM** — the old empty-`and`-group bug only bites ES/armour/life slots (a bow builds a valid 2-stat group either way), so a persistent 400 there = the VM hasn't pulled+restarted the new server. Redeploy main on the VM.
- 2026-06-26 (latest 2): **Gear Finder "Rank by real DPS" empty-result fix + no-visible-browser hardening.** User on a 50000-div budget got *"No in-budget candidates matched your current rolls — raise the budget"* — misleading: the trade search returned ZERO because the stat mins were floored at **100% of current rolls**, so a near-BIS item had to beat itself on the top stats simultaneously (budget was never the limit). Fix in `gear-finder.js` `realRank()`: floor stat mins at **70% of current rolls** (PoB ΔDPS still sorts the wider net honestly); rewrote the empty-state message ("…your current rolls may already be near best-in-slot"). Left the basic-search link's floor strict (you sort that page by hand). Also **hardened `smoke-test.js` against opening a visible browser**: dropped the full-`chrome.exe` fallback entirely (it flashes a focus-stealing window even headless) — `chromiumExe()` now returns only the windowless `chrome-headless-shell`, and `browserChecks()` skips if the shell is absent rather than launching full Chrome. Memory saved: always-commit/push/update-AGENTS, and never-open-a-visible-browser-tab.
- 2026-06-26 (latest): **Gear Finder — long iteration session, now genuinely usable on the VM.** Built on the headless-PoB engine: (1) **Split-host bridge LIVE** — `pob-agent.js` on the Main PC (under pm2 via `ecosystem.config.js`) + `pob.js` remote mode; VM reaches it via the PC's **Tailscale IP** (`POB_BRIDGE_URL` wired through compose). (2) **"Rank by real DPS"** is now the PRIMARY action (`/api/gear/realrank`: fetch in-budget candidates → score each in PoB → sort by actual ΔDPS) — the weighted *sum* search was a linear heuristic that recommended DPS downgrades. - 2026-06-25: **Trade2 record/replay layer (offline dev/testing) — declined IP rotation.** User asked to auto-rotate the VPN country to dodge the GGG limit "until the tool's done, then revert". Built the legit fix instead: **record/replay in `trade-queue.js`** (the single chokepoint for ALL Trade2). `POE_RECORD=1` captures real responses to `trade-fixtures.json` (sha1 of method+path+body); `POE_OFFLINE=1` replays them with ZERO network/budget (`/api/trade-status` → `replay:true`; a miss throws → graceful `found:false`). So the tool now develops + tests entirely offline. New convention bullet + `trade-queue-test.js` (4 checks). - 2026-06-25: **NEW TOOL — Jewel Pricer.** Rare jewels are combo-driven and mostly junk, so a per-mod `price:asc` floor just prices "a junk jewel sharing that mod" and they "don't cleanly show up on the scanner". Built (mirrors Map Juicer): paste 1+ rare jewels → OFFLINE triage (tier each mod, combo verdict, ZERO trade calls) → opt-in per-jewel **Price check** → `POST /api/jewel/price` (`getJewelFloor`) which ANDs the top 2-3 mods at their rolled floors under `category:jewel,rarity:nonunique` = "cheapest GOOD jewel like this", de-baited/clustered (reuses `getTradePrice`), returns `{ex,depth,thin}`.
