- 2026-06-11: Implemented "weighted sum" workaround for "total flat elemental" damage searching. Since GGG's PoE2 Trade API does not support the `sum` filter type for these mods, Gear Search now uses the `weight` filter group with a weight of 1 assigned to each component mod (Fire, Cold, Lightning, etc.). This forces the official Trade site to correctly sum the values and filter by the requested magnitude.
- Verification: `node --check server.js` passed. Trade queries now use the `weight` group with `value: { weight: 1 }` per filter and the user's requested minimum as the group total.
- 2026-06-13: REVERTED the `sum`/`weight` composite workarounds. Verified live against anonymous Trade2 that both `sum` and `weight` stat groups return HTTP 400 "Query is too complex. Logging in will increase this limit." — they require a logged-in session, which this tool does not use. The previous two commits (`f3744a5` sum, `69253f9` weight) had broken every combined flat-damage search (`totalFlatElementalAttack`, `totalFlatAttack`). Restored the broad `count` prefilter (`value: { min: 1 }`, require >=1 component present) and rely on the existing local post-filter (`postValue` + `compositeStatsSatisfied`, fetch up to 60 candidates) to enforce the true combined min/max. Also removed a leftover `console.log("TRADE QUERY:")` debug line in `searchGear`.

- 2026-06-13: Added per-listing "View on Trade" deep-ish link to Gear Search. Each `/api/gear-search/search` listing now carries a compact `tradeSpec` (category, exact price, top explicit stat mins). New endpoint `POST /api/gear-search/listing-link` builds a focused, price-sorted Trade2 search for that single item and returns its URL (status `any` so offline sellers still show). Front-end adds a "View on Trade" button per listing that opens the official PoE2 UI on that search. GGG has no true single-listing permalink, so this surfaces the item near the top of a tight search rather than in isolation.
  - Spec excludes aggregation-prone keys: derived totals, equipment props (ev/es/dps/deflection), and fire/cold/lightning res + str/dex/int (the parser folds "all elemental res"/"all attributes" into those, which would otherwise exclude the item from its own search). chaosRes kept. - 2026-06-13: Added listing freshness + seller-status indicators to Gear Search (helps spot stale listings — seller online but item already sold). `searchGear` listings now include `sellerStatus` (online/afk/dnd/offline, derived from `listing.account.online` via `sellerOnlineStatus`); `listedAt` (existing `listing.indexed`) is now rendered as a relative "x ago" badge instead of a raw ISO string. Front-end shows colored badges: seller status (green online / gold afk-dnd / muted offline) and age (green <1h fresh, red >=12h stale). Both come from data already in the fetch response — no extra Trade2 calls. Badge tooltip notes status is the seller account, not live item availability (GGG exposes no real-time in-stash flag). - 2026-06-13: Baked MARKET-DERIVED mod values into Map Juicer. Used the Trade2 API's dedicated waystone `map_filters` (`map_packsize`, `map_iir`, `map_rare_monsters`, `map_magic_monsters`, `map_tier`; category `map.waystone`) to run a one-off Tier-16 price-floor sweep (cheapest exalted-priced listing at each stat threshold = market's marginal price for that roll). Findings: **Pack Size ≈ Monster Effectiveness ≫ Item Rarity (pays only ≥50%) ≫ Monster Rarity (~6ex flat).** Pack≥35 floors ~40ex; Rarity≥35 ~2-6ex. Also confirmed a 0.5 reality: **waystones have NO "Quantity of Items" stat** (gone; reward axes are Item Rarity, Pack Size, Monster Rarity, Monster Effectiveness, + Drop Chance sustain) and at T16 essentially every *listed* waystone is corrupted. Baked into `waystone-data.js`: new `marketWeights` block (source/date/per-stat weight+premiumAt+floors+tip, weight normalised to Pack Size=1.0), reordered `waystoneTargets` by market value with target %s, fixed `tokens` (dropped invalid `uantit`, lead Pack Size). In `waystone-juicer.html`: new "Mod value — what the market pays for" card (ranked bars), market-led run regex (`"ack s" "agic monst|onster eff|rar"`), and the paste-evaluator now computes a weighted **market value score** (Σ weight×rolled%) + best stat, so a pack-heavy map scores "premium" even with low rarity and a pure-rarity map is flagged cheap-to-make. Handles both copy formats ("38% increased Pack Size" and "Pack Size: +35%"). Still offline at runtime — weights are statically baked, re-run the sweep per patch. Mind the shared Trade2 rate limit when re-sweeping (I tripped it once mid-run; the queue recovered).

Server serves /waystone-juicer.html and /waystone-data.js (200). Temp probe scripts removed.
- 2026-06-13: Added an in-tool "Refresh from market" button to Map Juicer (live re-sweep of mod weights, replacing reliance on the static bake). Backend: `GET /api/waystone/market-weights` returns the file-cached weights (no trade calls); `POST /api/waystone/market-weights/refresh` runs `runWaystoneSweep` through the shared adaptive Trade2 queue (7 searches incl. baseline → `waystoneFloor` reads cheapest exalted Tier-16 listing per stat threshold; `robustWaystoneFloor` takes the 2nd-cheapest when the cheapest is <½ of it to dodge AFK/mispriced 1ex listings; weights normalised to the top stat, `premiumAt` = lowest threshold ≥3× baseline & ≥10ex). Guards: returns `{limited}` if the queue is blocked, a 10-min `{cooldown}` unless `force:true`, and NEVER overwrites a good cache on a partial/rate-limited sweep. Result cached to `.waystone-weights.json` (gitignored). Front-end: market card shows a `live`/`baked` tag + Refresh button + status line; `loadCachedWeights()` picks up server cache on load (graceful no-op when served statically); `MW()` overrides the baked `D.marketWeights` when live weights are present. Live run verified: Pack Size weight 1.0 (40ex @35%), Monster Effectiveness/Item Rarity ~0.5, Monster Rarity 0.03 — ranking matches the baked bake. Cooldown + GET paths confirmed to make zero trade calls.

- 2026-06-13: Map Juicer evaluator now (a) shows an approximate VALUE for both item kinds and (b) suggests the best-fit CONTENT TYPE. New `contentFit(rolls)` normalises each rolled % by its ceiling, scores every content type, and returns a ranking; the evaluator appends "Best for <content> (<driver stat>-heavy) — socket <content> tablets" (+ a close runner-up). Waystones show "Est. floor value ≈ N ex" (from the baked %-curve, no live trade needed); tablets show an "Approx. value Strong/Decent/Light/Weak" band from roll-quality vs ceilings plus "This is a <content> tablet". Evaluator was already type-agnostic (parses pasted text only, not the active tab). No server.js change (static files served fresh).
- 2026-06-13: CORRECTED the Map Juicer mod-value model to be %-AWARE (price-vs-% curve per stat) after realising the earlier flat per-stat weight was biased. The bias: comparing stats at the same ABSOLUTE % (pack≥35 vs rarity≥35) is unfair because roll CEILINGS differ — Pack Size maxes ~41%, Item Rarity rolls to ~84%. A finer sweep (floor at multiple %s per stat) flipped the headline: **Item Rarity has by far the highest ceiling and its price EXPLODES at the top — 30%→1ex, 50%→20ex, 70%→~325ex (~8× the best Pack Size roll).** Pack Size 20%→1ex, 30%→20ex, 40%→40ex (caps ~40); Monster Effectiveness 20%→1ex, 40%→37ex; Monster Rarity ~1ex even at ≥40%. So: at MID rolls Pack/Meff are worth more per % (~2ex/% vs rarity ~1ex/%), but at HIGH rolls Rarity wins massively (~15ex/% from 50→70 and keeps climbing). Reworked `marketWeights` in waystone-data.js to carry a `curve:[[pct,ex]]` + `ceiling` + `peakEx` per stat (ranked by peak: Rarity > Pack ≈ Meff > MonsterRarity), reordered `waystoneTargets`, and rewrote the evaluator: `curveEx()` interpolates/extrapolates a stat's ex floor at the rolled %, and a map's headline value ≈ its single BEST stat (floors are whole-map, not summed) — so a near-max pure-Rarity map now reads premium (~400ex) where the old flat model wrongly scored it ~33. Market card now shows each stat's curve + ceiling (log-scaled bar so 325 doesn't crush 40) instead of a single weight bar. Server `runWaystoneSweep` updated to the same shape with finer thresholds (Rarity 30/50/70, Pack 20/30/40, Meff 20/40, MRare 40 = 10 searches) and reads each listing's rolled prop to derive `ceiling`; front-end `loadCachedWeights` now ignores old-format caches (requires `stats[0].curve`). Deleted the stale `.waystone-weights.json` so baked curves show until a live Refresh repopulates.
- Verification (2026-06-13): finer live sweep ran clean (rarity≥70 → 325ex floor over 100 listings was the standout). `node --check` on server.js + data.js + inline script all pass. Node-tested curve scoring: pure-rarity 75% → ~401ex (premium), max-pack40+meff35 → 40ex, mid-pack30+rarity40 → 20ex (pack wins mid), mid-rarity45 → 15ex, junk → 1ex. Server restarted; GET weights → null (baked curves show); page 200.

- 2026-06-13: Critically reviewed + fixed Codex's Arbitrage Scanner (root cause of the chronic rate-limiting). THE bug: the front-end `payload()` hardcoded `force:true`, so every Scan bypassed the 2-min cache and ran a full live sweep; combined with ~22 Trade2 calls per scan (2 exchange calls × 11 items) it tripped the shared limit constantly. Fixes: (1) `force` is now an opt-in "Force live refresh" checkbox (default off) — repeat scans return the cache in ~0.15s with ZERO trade calls. (2) Replaced per-item fetching with chunked batched exchange queries: `have`/`want` accept arrays, but the API rejects ≥~11 ("Too many items") AND a wide batch returns a capped page that starves currencies (a 9-want buy dropped Divine entirely). Verified a 3-wide batch covers every currency, so `fetchExchangeChunked` chunks the multi-currency side at `EXCHANGE_BATCH_CAP=3` and merges offer maps — ~8 calls per full scan vs 22, queue tied up ~25s vs ~165s. (3) Empty-state now says "Scanned N pairs — spread is usually negative for instant round-trips…" so a no-arbitrage result doesn't read as broken. Confirmed all 11 official static tags are valid (currency + both splinters); the earlier missing-items were coverage, not bad ids. Kept Codex's limit-timestamp UI.

Forced scan (cap 3, both categories): universe 11, no rate-limit, ~8 calls (~42s), 9/11 covered (Regal + Simulacrum Splinter thin/page-starved, low liquidity), 0 profitable opportunities = correct (Exchange spread is negative for instant flips). Zero-risk as predicted (CSS already prefix-scoped, JS already lazy `__viewInit` fns); smoke test 37/37 after the move. To add a tool: a `.css`, a `.js` (wrap in `window.__viewInit["<view>"]=function(){…}`), a `<section class="view toolroot-<x>">` in index, a nav link, and the two `<link>`/`<script src>` tags.
- HOW TO FIX THE MONOLITH (DONE 2026-06-14 — see above; kept for reference) — was: index.html ~2000 lines — recommended, zero-risk because tool CSS is already prefix-scoped (`.toolroot-x`) and tool JS is already isolated lazy fns: (1) Move each tool's `.toolroot-x …` CSS block out of index's `<style>` into its own file (`arbitrage.css`/`map-juicer.css`/`gear-search.css`, or one `tools.css`) and `<link>` it after theme.css — cascade is unchanged (specificity, not order, is what makes `.toolroot-x` win). (2) Move Arbitrage's + Map Juicer's `window.__viewInit["x"]=function(){…}` into `arbitrage.js`/`map-juicer.js` and `<script src>` them before `</body>`, exactly like the existing `gear-search.js` — the registry + DOMContentLoaded init already handle them regardless of file. (3) KEEP the view markup inline (HTML can't be linked without a build step or a fetch-include + flash; markup is the small part). Result: index ≈ shell markup + main app script (~700 lines); each tool = 1 css + 1 js + a `<section>`. Run `node smoke-test.js` after to confirm nothing moved wrong. (NOT a build step — preserves the zero-build edit-and-refresh workflow.)

- 2026-06-14: **Adaptive backfill for exchange page-starvation** (`fetchExchangeChunked`, server.js). A high-liquidity currency (Divine) in a 3-wide chunk can fill the single capped response page and starve its chunk-mates of offers. After the batched pass, the fn now re-fetches any item that came back with ZERO offers, ALONE (its own page), bounded by `EXCHANGE_BACKFILL_CAP=6` and skipped entirely on an empty merged (rate-limit/systemic failure, not starvation) so it can't burst. Benefits both the arbitrage scan and currency-rate sweep. **Made server.js requireable** for tests: `server.listen` is now guarded by `require.main === module`, and it exports `{fetchExchangeChunked, collectExchangeOffers, bestExchangeOffer, __setExchangeRawImpl}` (the latter injects a stubbed network). New `backfill-test.js` exercises the REAL code with a stubbed whale-starvation page (9 assertions: every starved item recovered, whale not re-fetched, zero waste when nothing starved) — wired into smoke as a static check, **75/75**. Verified live (careful, spaced, queue self-throttled, never tripped the limit): a forced scan ran clean (HTTP 200, not limited); at `minStock:1` coverage is 9/11 with only Regal Orb + Simulacrum Splinter missing — and they're missing at presence-level too, i.e. today they genuinely have NO exalted-pair offer one side (a real market gap, NOT page starvation the backfill can fix). So the fix is a correctness/robustness improvement proven by the offline determinism test; it can't manufacture offers that don't exist.
- 2026-06-14: Home currency strip degrades gracefully when there are no rates (`home.js`). Previously `render()` set `strip.hidden=true` on empty `items`, so on a fresh VM (cold cache whose first live fetch hit the Trade2 limit) the strip VANISHED — looked broken AND removed the ↻ button (the only retry path). Now an empty-but-responding result keeps the strip visible with a "No currency rates yet" chip + a "Trade2 rate-limited / unavailable — tap ↻ to retry" meta. True fetch failures (static host, no server) are still caught in `load()` and hide it. Smoke +1 (empty/limited mock → strip stays visible + retryable), **76/76**. (Diagnostic for the field: hit `/api/currency/overview?league=Runes%20of%20Aldur` — `items:[]`+`limited:true` = IP rate-limited, will populate on ↻ once clear; empty without `limited` = transient/unreachable.)
- 2026-06-14: **`sanitizeLeague` — defensive league cleaning** (server.js). A reverse proxy in front of the deployed VM (`docker:8098`) was appending its own origin onto the `league` query value, so the server received `"Runes of Aldurhttp://docker:8098"` → that went straight into the GGG exchange URL → **HTTP 400 "Invalid query"** → empty currency rates → the home strip showed nothing. Added `sanitizeLeague(raw)`: cuts at an embedded `http(s)://`, strips to PoE-league chars (`[A-Za-z0-9 '-]`), collapses whitespace, falls back to `DEFAULT_LEAGUE`. Applied at all 6 GET `?league=` handlers and the two URL-building chokepoints (`getExchangeData`, `scanArbitrage`), so no caller can push a junk league into an upstream API. Exported + unit-tested in `backfill-test.js` (4 assertions: strips proxy origin, leaves clean league, empty→default, trims). NOTE: this is server-side hardening; the user's proxy still mangles the query and should be fixed too (it may corrupt other params). Smoke 76/76 (backfill-test now 13 assertions).

- 2026-06-14: **Fixed Rune Picker slowness — stale-while-revalidate + background warming** for the Trade2 currency cache. Root cause: moving currency pricing onto the Trade2 exchange made `getExchangeData` BLOCK the user whenever the 10-min cache was stale (a live chunked fetch through the 30s-gap queue = 30-90s). For a low-traffic single user the cache is stale most checks, so the Rune Picker (which calls `getExchangeData` for currency rates) felt "super slow." Fix: `getExchangeData` now NEVER blocks except the explicit ↻ (force) and a true cold start — a stale cache is returned instantly (`stale:true`) while a single-flight `refreshExchangeData` updates it in the background. Added `warmExchange()` on a 2-min interval (only refreshes when the cache is within 2 min of TTL; single-flight + rate-limit aware) so the cache stays warm without user traffic. Live-verified: stale 17-min cache served `/api/currency/overview` in **4ms** (was a 30-90s block) and the bg refresh completed ~20s later; `/api/rune-prices` (runes + Divine/Exalted) returns in **~30-90ms**, correct (Trade2 currency + poe.ninja runes). Smoke 76/76. (Still open: runes/essences/soul cores price from poe.ninja which the user finds inaccurate — next is moving those onto Trade2 via the same cached-snapshot approach.)
- 2026-06-15: **Rune Picker accuracy — Trade2 exchange price book (fills poe.ninja's gaps), fast.** poe.ninja's PoE2 coverage of runes/essences/soul cores is thin ("useless for most stuff" — e.g. it can't price Soul Cores at all). Probed the Trade2 static catalog: Runes (213), Essences (84), Soul Cores (Vaal, 47) etc. are ALL on the bulk exchange. So: `buildExchangeCatalog` walks `data/static` into a normName→{id,name,category} map (stored on `arbitrageStaticCache.catalog`, 1h); `fetchRunePrices` now consults a persistent **price book** (`.rune-exchange-book.json`, gitignored) keyed by normName. **HYBRID precedence** (deliberate): poe.ninja keeps the win where it has a real volume-weighted price (it's FINER for cheap sub-1ex items, and the exchange is coarse/noisy there — using it everywhere flipped cheap-rune rankings in testing); the Trade2 book is used ONLY when poe.ninja has no usable price (the actual coverage gap). NEVER blocks: the book serves instantly; pasted items that are missing/stale in the book (>30min) trigger a single-flight BACKGROUND batched-exchange fill (`refreshRuneBook` → `fetchExchangeChunked` + `bestExchangeOffer`), so the book fills from real usage and the NEXT check is accurate. Items with no exalted-side exchange offer just stay on poe.ninja. Live-verified: 1st check 216ms (poe.ninja + Soul Core "NOT FOUND"), bg fill wrote 4 entries incl. the soul core, 2nd check 30-99ms with Soul Core now `trade2 exchange` while cheap Lesser runes correctly kept poe.ninja's granular prices (ranking preserved). `buildExchangeCatalog` exported + unit-tested (3 asserts in backfill-test.js). Smoke 76/76. (Knob if the user wants Trade2-everywhere instead of hybrid: prefer `bookResultFor` before the poe.ninja branch.)

- 2026-06-15: **Rune Picker pricing-accuracy pass** (4 commits `df435df`→`7c656bb`, smoke 84→85). Refined WHEN the live Trade2 exchange should beat poe.ninja, plus two correctness fixes. (1) `df435df`: the "Fetch fresh prices" button now PREFERS the live Trade2 book per pasted item (was still rendering poe.ninja because hybrid precedence gave poe.ninja the win wherever it had a price — so a force visibly did nothing); falls back to poe.ninja only where the exchange has no offer. (2) `cd29fa6`: **liquidity-gate** the forced override — only beat poe.ninja with the live price when book `stock >= RUNE_FRESH_MIN_STOCK` (default **30**); the bulk exchange is an order book and cheap runes often have 5-11 units standing, so the cheapest offer is noise (e.g. 5ex for a 0.4ex rune) vs poe.ninja's volume-weighted aggregate. (4) `7c656bb`: **utility currencies price instead of NOT FOUND** — Blacksmith's Whetstone / Arcanist's Etcher / Armourer's Scrap sit in the catalog's "Currency" group and `refreshRuneBook` skipped the WHOLE group (to avoid double-pricing the curated main currencies `getExchangeData` handles); now it skips only the **curated currency ids** `getExchangeData` actually prices (from `resolveArbitrageItems`), so the book covers runes/essences/soul cores AND uncurated utility currencies. New knobs: `RUNE_FRESH_MIN_STOCK` (30), `RUNE_FRESH_DEADLINE_MS` (35s). All live-verified per commit; all pushed.
- 2026-06-15: **Fixed user-reported "Divine price is off"** (currency strip showed Divine = 1.00 ex instead of ~150, hero "1.00 ex PER DIVINE", and Chaos/Annul/Chance/Fracturing mis-rendered "in div" because `home.js` divides by `divineEx`=1; Vaal & Gemcutter's Prism also read 1.00 ex). Root cause (proven by a live exchange-offer probe): the bulk Currency Exchange is littered with spam **"par" listings** swapping the base unit one-for-one — `1 exalted : 1 divine`, often with real stock — and `bestExchangeOffer` took the cheapest offer above the stock floor, so the par junk (ratio 1) beat the real ~166-185ex floor → rate 1. Fix in `server.js`: new `robustCheapestOffer` drops offers where `payAmount === receiveAmount` (the par signature; no legit seller offers a par swap vs exalted) and takes the cheapest *real* one, falling back to par only if nothing else exists; `bestExchangeOffer` now routes through it. Deliberately NOT a median/outlier filter — that was tried first and WRONGLY repriced sub-1ex high-liquidity currencies (Aug 0.14→4.95) because the many par-junk offers drag the median up to 1; sub-1ex currencies already pick their true floor below the par junk, so par-drop leaves them untouched. Helps all 3 callers (strip rate, arbitrage buy-leg — par junk would fabricate a ~149ex fake Divine arbitrage, rune book). Live-verified: Divine 1→166, Vaal 1→4, GCP 1→2, Chaos 13 unchanged, Transmute 0.333 preserved. Regression test in `backfill-test.js` (+3 asserts, 16→19). smoke 85/85. (At fix time the shared Trade2 IP was rate-limited from the diagnostic probes, so the cache couldn't refresh immediately — it self-corrects on the next successful refresh; deploy with `--build`.)

- 2026-06-15: **Gear Search — slot-aware stat-id resolution (weapon/quiver crit + attack speed were dead filters).** Root cause (user-reported, then proven live against the Trade2 stat dictionary + real listing counts): the tool had ONE flat key→id map (`UPGRADE_STAT_IDS`) but in PoE2 the SAME concept has DIFFERENT trade ids per slot — crit/AS are *weapon-local* on weapons, "*for Attacks*"/"*for Attack Damage*" on quivers, and generic on amulets/jewels. So a bow searched for `critChance` (global `587431675`) or `attackSpeed` (global `681332047`) hit ids weapons can't roll → **0 results** (proven: bow global crit 0 listings vs local `518292764` 6278; global AS 0 vs local `210067635` 5989; bow crit-dmg is "to Crit Damage Bonus" `2694482655` 4340; quiver crit-dmg is "for Attack Damage" `3714003708`). Fix: new `SLOT_STAT_OVERRIDES` (bow: critChance→`518292764`, critDamage→`2694482655`, attackSpeed→`210067635`; quiver: critDamage→`3714003708`) + `gearStatId(key,slot)` resolver (override→generic fallback), used at the real query-build site (`buildGearSearchStatFilters`). Parser broadened to capture all three crit-damage texts into one `critDamage` key, and the weapon's *base* "Critical Hit Chance: X%" property moved to a display-only `critChanceBase` so it can't poison the searchable `critChance` filter (was making bows without a crit mod search the +%-to-crit id at a 6.5 base → 0). Bow's exposed key list: dropped dead `attackSpeed` (DPS already encodes AS for weapons), added `critDamage`+`localPhysDamage`. Armour/accessories unaffected (resolver returns generic). Verified live: a bow crit search that returned **0 → 20 listings**; preview ids correct for bow+quiver; smoke 85/85. KNOWN: override table is hand-maintained (re-hit when more weapons are added — see multi-weapon work); bow attack-speed roll no longer filterable on its own (DPS covers it).
- 2026-06-15: **Gear Search — usable search defaults (import+search returned near-nothing).** Match mode defaulted to **All filters** AND `setDefaultFilters` pre-filled each filter's min to the item's EXACT current roll, so a search ANDed ~6–10 stats each at your current value → only matched items strictly ≥ you on EVERY axis → almost always 0 (proven live: a real bow filter set = 0 in "all" vs **171 total / 20 fetched** in "count ≥3"). Fix: default match mode → **"Match at least N"** (count), and `setDefaultFilters` auto-sets `minMatches = max(1, round(filterCount*0.6))` (server caps to the non-composite filter count); user can still tighten to "All filters". Also deleted a DEAD duplicate stat-id map in `gear-search.js` (`STAT_IDS`, defined-but-never-referenced, still holding the old wrong crit/AS ids) — server is the single source of truth and the front end only sends `{key,min,max}`. smoke 85/85.
- 2026-06-15: **Gear Search — 0-result diagnosis.** Empty searches showed a bare "No priced listings returned" with no cause. New `emptyStateHtml(result)` (gear-search.js) distinguishes the cases from the response fields: `total === 0` → "filters too strict" + concrete relax tips (lower **Match at least N** "now K of M", or switch off All-filters, remove a filter, lower Mins); `total > 0` but nothing priced/in view → "matched on Trade but priced out — raise Budget / inspect on Trade" (+ a note when a combined flat-damage local post-filter is active); always lists any `unsupportedFilters` that were dropped. Keeps the Open-on-Trade link. smoke +1 (mock total=0, count mode 3 of 4 → asserts the diagnostic + relax hint render) → **86/86**.
- 2026-06-15: **Gear Search — multi-weapon support (was bow-only).** The profile defined only `bow`, so no other weapon could be searched. Added every real PoE2 0.5 weapon class via one compact injected table (`EXTRA_WEAPON_SLOTS`, categories from the live Trade2 category list): martial 1H (claw, dagger, onesword, oneaxe, onemace, spear, flail), martial 2H (twosword, twoaxe, twomace, quarterstaff=`weapon.warstaff`), ranged (crossbow), caster (wand, staff, sceptre). **Martial weapons all share the SAME weapon-LOCAL stat ids** (verified live: bow + spear identical — localPhys `1509134228`, "to crit chance" `518292764`, "to crit dmg" `2694482655`, local AS `210067635`, flats), so they reuse bow's filter set + bow's `SLOT_STAT_OVERRIDES`. **Caster weapons** use a spell stat set (`spellDamage 2974417149`, `castSpeed 2891184298`, `levelAllSpellSkills 124131830`, `mana 1050105434`, `manaRegen 789117908`) with crit redirected to the SPELL variants (`critChance→737908626`, `critDamage→274716455`) via a caster override; **sceptres** get a minion/spirit set (`spirit`, `spiritPct 3984865854`, mana, manaRegen, int, `levelAllMinionSkills 2162097452`). Added new caster stat ids + parser regexes (spell damage / cast speed / +spell&minion levels / mana / mana regen / %spirit / spell-crit), `SLOT_ALIASES` Item-Class detection for each class (anchored to `Item Class:` so "Staves" can't match "Quarterstaves"), and labels. Front-end `renderSlots` now lists imported slots first (●) so the ~25-slot dropdown isn't a wall of weapons. Verified live: spear/wand/sceptre searches return real listings (1957/2679/3188 totals), spear→weapon-local crit ids, wand→spell crit ids + spell damage. Exported `analyzeGearSearch`/`buildGearSearchQuery`/`gearSearchSlots`; backfill-test +6 (19→**25**: slot exposure, spear-local vs wand-spell vs amulet-generic crit resolution, spear/wand detection). smoke 86/86. KNOWN: martial classes share local ids by design (only bow+spear verified live, but local mods are slot-agnostic); caster parser covers core mods but not every niche caster affix; the guided import wizard still only has a "Bow" box (other weapons go through Advanced raw import, which detects them); in-game `Item Class:` strings for swords/axes were not paste-verified (regexes are tolerant; confirm with a real item).

- 2026-06-15: **Gear Search P0 fixes (from the ruthless self-critique).** (1) **"Match at least N" was silently collapsing to strict AND for real weapons.** The front end computed N from the UI ROW count, but the server's count group excludes `dps` (an equipment_filter) and composite groups — so a typical 8-row elemental bow → N=5 over a 5-filter count group = AND (0 results). Fixed: the SERVER now computes `matchMin = max(1, round(countGroupSize*0.6))` from the real `queryFilters.length` (round(0.6n) ≤ n-1 for n≥2, so never strict); front end leaves Min count BLANK (auto) and only sends a number when the user types one; response carries `matchMin`/`matchOf`, shown in the summary ("Match ≥2 of 4") + as the input placeholder. (2) **Gear Search only showed divine-listed items.** `trade_filters.price.option:"divine"` made Trade2 return ONLY divine-listed listings — hiding ~80% of the market (proven live: bow crit total 1057 with the filter vs **4962** without; every result was "1 divine", never an exalt listing). Removed the currency price filter entirely; sort price-asc (Trade2 converts across currencies) and enforce the **budget LOCALLY** on the converted exalted value in `searchGear` (skipped when no divine rate, so it can't wrongly hide everything). Live-verified: loose bow search now total 4962 with mixed currencies ("1 aug / 1 transmute / …") and a 0.5-div budget trims correctly. backfill-test +5 (28→**33**: count group excludes dps/composites, auto-min relaxed, query encodes it, user-min capped, no trade_filters). smoke 86/86. (Minor: the very first live search right after a server restart can return empty while the exchange-rate cache warms — pre-existing `getExchangeRates` cold-start, harmless on a long-running server.)

- 2026-06-15: **Gear Search — accurate per-slot affix pools (the big one).** Root cause of "a bow offers Cold Resistance": `filterOptions` (gear-search.js) appended `life + all resistances + rarity` to EVERY slot's list. HONEST GAPS: pools cover the tool's ~50 supported keys (not every niche affix); a few inclusions lean on PoE2 rules where the small live sample didn't surface them (e.g. amulet spellDamage); belt flat-armour intentionally omitted (no armour property to filter via `ar`); base-type nuance not modeled (an ES helmet vs armour helmet share one pool — the dropdown offers all three defence types, defaults derive from the item's actual rolls).

- 2026-06-19: **Rune Picker — fixed "never really scans trade".** Diagnosed live: the Trade2 exchange mechanism was fine (a clean `fetchExchangeChunked("exalted",["desert-rune"])` returns real offers; real Soul Cores/essences/runes ARE in the static catalog with valid exchange-ids, e.g. `soul core of tacati → soul-core-of-tacati`), but the price book (`.rune-exchange-book.json`) stayed EMPTY because the fill kept losing to the shared Trade2 rate limit and failing **silently**. Two root causes + fixes in `server.js`: (1) **forceFresh fired two heavy queue ops concurrently** — `Promise.allSettled([refreshRuneBook(force), getExchangeData(force)])` — which doubled the burst and routinely self-tripped the rate limit, so the forced refresh wrote nothing and returned at the 35s deadline. Now it awaits ONLY `refreshRuneBook` (the divine rate is served stale-while-revalidate by the normal `getExchangeData(league)` below, no forced sweep). (2) **The forced "Fetch fresh prices" button was gated by `RUNE_FRESH_MIN_STOCK=30`** so it kept poe.ninja for any item with thin book depth — i.e. the button visibly did nothing for normal runes. Dropped the gate on the explicit force: an explicit force now prefers the live book price whenever present (stock + confidence badge are shown in the row so the user judges noise); removed the now-dead `RUNE_FRESH_MIN_STOCK` const. The DEFAULT "Check picks" still keeps poe.ninja's finer volume-weighted price where it has one and only uses the book for true coverage gaps (soul cores). Live-verified end-to-end (spaced, no limit): a forced check of `Soul Core of Tacati / Desert Rune / Greater Essence of Flames` returned in **8s** (was 35s) with all three priced `trade2 exchange` + stock, and the book filled to 27 entries; the same default check kept Soul Core on trade2 (gap) while Desert Rune/essence stayed on poe.ninja's finer price. smoke 86/86. (Background note: the book accumulates across checks via the existing fire-and-forget `refreshRuneBook(stale)`; it just needed to stop racing itself into the rate limit.)

- 2026-06-19: **Economy dashboard — fixed wrong prices for omens & Hinekora's Lock** (user-reported). Root cause: `sampleEconomy` priced EVERY item vs EXALTED, with a divine fallback only when the exalted side returned *nothing*. But high-value items (omens, Hinekora's Lock) have junk lowball offers on the exalted side (1-stock scams, e.g. Hinekora's = 5ex) that won, so the divine fallback never fired. The real liquid market for these is the **DIVINE side** of the same bulk exchange (= the in-game currency exchange the user checks: Hinekora's ≈ **680 div**, confirmed live, matching the user's ~665). Fix: flag those items `div: true` in `ECONOMY_ITEMS` and price them against divine via new `cheapestDivineOffer(data, wantId, minStock)` — cheapest divine-per-item across divine-side offers with item-stock ≥2 (skips 1-stock lowballs), ×exPerDiv → ex. Needed a dedicated helper because `bestExchangeOffer` is exalted-oriented: it checks the wrong stock side for have=divine queries and its par-filter would drop legit `1 div : 1 omen` offers. Liquid currency (Divine, Greater/Perfect Exalted, Mirror) still prices vs exalted. **Detour corrected mid-session:** I first concluded the exchange was junk for these and routed them through the regular item trade search (`tradeSearchMedianEx`, median of cheapest listings) — that source is full of scam lowballs/highballs (5ex floor, "1 mirror" highs) and the "exchange is junk" read came from a flaky **rate-limited 0-offers response**; re-probing cleanly showed the divine side has real depth (36-48 offers). Reverted the item-search path entirely. Live-verified: Hinekora's 680 div, omens ~1 div each, Mirror 52.8 div; reset `.economy-history.json` to one clean point (old points used the broken pricing → not comparable). smoke **89/89**. Memory: `economy-price-high-value-against-divine`. - 2026-06-20: **Economy + Rune Picker unified on one robust exchange estimator** (user: economy showed divine 165/stale, greater-exalt 49.95, etc.; "the currency strip is closer — shouldn't both pull the same source, both current?"; and Rune Picker priced Orb of Alchemy at 16ex + missed items like Thrud's Might). Three fixes in `server.js` + `home.js`:
  - **(1) Pricing estimator — clustering replaces the quarter-of-median floor** (`robustCheapestOffer`). Root cause of BOTH the divine-too-low and alch-too-high errors: the old "drop par, reject below ¼·median, take cheapest" floor let a **lone lowball bait** through (divine had one `165ex:1div` stock-7 offer above a real cluster at 215–300 → resolved 165, real ~250) AND, in reverse, cut the **real cheap fills** of cheap currencies as "bait" (alch's genuine 1.2–4.95ex offers sit below ¼·median≈5, so it landed on 15/16). New rule = the cheapest offer that sits in a **CLUSTER** (≥3 peers within ±15%, the same robust rule the divine-side `divineMarketPrice` already used); lone baits/walls have no cluster and are skipped; thin books (<4 real offers) still fall back to cheapest. Live-verified: divine 165→**249**, alch 16→**1.2**, chaos 21, greater-exalt 49.95 (its book genuinely clusters at 45–50 — nothing fillable near the user's eyeballed "4"; illiquid, can't fix without item-search). This touches EVERYTHING through `bestExchangeOffer` (strip, arbitrage, rune book) — strictly better than the floor (it catches the 165 the floor missed).
  - **(2) Economy panel now shows CURRENT, shared with the strip** (the "same source, both current" ask). Was rendering the last twice-a-day history point (up to 12h stale, and the stored point was pre-fix old-code w/ a `mirror` the code no longer samples). Added `economyCurrent(league)`: exalt-side items (Divine, **Greater/Perfect Exalted — now added to `ARBITRAGE_ITEMS` as rate-only so the strip's shared `getExchangeData` prices them in ONE call**, and they show as strip chips) read straight off the same live 10-min-SWR rates the strip renders → a shared price like Divine is byte-identical in both and refreshes together; div-side items (omens/Hinekora's, not on the strip) use a new SWR-cached `economyDivSide` (10-min TTL, in-memory) anchored to that same live Divine. `/api/economy/history` returns `current` alongside `points`; `home.js` renders headline+cards off `current`, history `points` only drive the trend graph + "% vs start". History sampling stays 12h (a trend graph is inherently sampled).
  - **(3) Rune Picker "Check picks" no longer misses booked-able items.** Default check read the book as-is → un-booked items (e.g. Thrud's Might, a rune that IS on the exchange) showed NOT FOUND until you separately hit "Fetch fresh". Now the default fills the book INLINE for missing/stale pasted items before pricing (bounded by `RUNE_FRESH_DEADLINE_MS`); stays instant when the book's warm; "Fetch fresh" still force-refetches everything. Live-verified with a **cold book**: one default click priced Thrud's Might (65ex), Chaos (21), alch (1.2) — no NOT FOUND. Currency rewards already priced off `getExchangeData` (so already unified); the estimator fix is what corrected the numbers.
  - Verification: `node --check` ✓, smoke **90/90**, screenshot-confirmed home (hero + economy both 249 ex/Div, strip carries Greater/Perfect Exalted chips). - 2026-06-21: **Currency pricing — the cheap/illiquid tier is unreliable off the order book; band-aid + the real fix identified.** User caught the strip/economy mispricing cheap currencies by 14-300x (Transmute 30ex vs a true ~0.1, Greater Exalted 44 vs ~3, Aug 30 vs ~0.4, Chance 45 vs ~10) while liquid staples (Divine/Chaos/Alch) were ~right. **Root cause (proven):** GGG's in-game "Market Ratio" is its own traded-data figure that is NOT in the standing order book we read — e.g. Greater Exalted's true 3.12 rate appears nowhere in its offers (cheapest ask is a lone 1:1 then a jump to 10, deep liquidity all on the bid side). Every order-book estimator (median-floor, clustering, one-sided-deep, two-sided geo-mid) swings 2-20x AND drifts day to day; none reproduces GGG's number. **(1) Band-aid shipped** (`server.js` `fetchExchangeData`): `TWO_SIDED_IDS = {transmute, aug, greater-exalted-orb}` are priced by `geoMidRate()` = geometric mid of the robust deep bid and deep ask (cheapest ask with stock>=5, NOT the cluster — the cluster IS the overpriced wall; bid = highest non-crossed buy offer). Turns the 75-300x catastrophes into ~2x. Costs one extra bid-side exchange call per id (3 total). Liquid staples stay one-sided (geo-mid would wrongly drag them to their lowball bids). **Perfect Exalted deliberately NOT in the set** — its book is 1-2 offers so two-sided gave 200 vs ~660 where one-sided gave ~560. It's a band-aid, honestly ~2-3x and wobbly, not accurate. **(2) THE REAL FIX = GGG cxapi.** Official endpoint `GET https://api.pathofexile.com/currency-exchange/poe2` (auth `service:cxapi`, client_credentials grant, token never expires) returns hourly per-market `lowest_ratio`/`highest_ratio`/`volume_traded` = exact traded ratios for every pair in ONE call, on a separate API host (doesn't touch the trade2 rate limit). The tool already has OAuth plumbing (`POE_CLIENT_ID`/`POE_CLIENT_SECRET`, confidential client). BLOCKER: `service:cxapi` isn't self-serve on /my-account/applications — must be requested by emailing **oauth@grindinggear.com** (GGG calls these low-priority). User is sending that email. **NEXT when scope granted:** build a cxapi client (client_credentials token fetch + cache, parse `currency-exchange/poe2` ratios into the currency rates), route the strip/economy/rune-currency pricing through it, keep the order-book path (incl. the geo-mid band-aid) as the automatic fallback, then DELETE `TWO_SIDED_IDS`/`geoMidRate`. Rune Picker NOT-FOUND reports (Thrud's Might, Astrid's Creativity, Medved's Saga) are all the SAME thing — booked-able exchange items that show NOT FOUND only when the cold-book inline fill hits its 35s deadline on a slow-queue pass; NOT the apostrophe. Open follow-up: make a catalog item that isn't booked yet show "pricing…/pending" instead of "NOT FOUND" (reserve NOT FOUND for genuinely off-exchange items that item-search also misses).
- 2026-06-21: **Rune Picker — fixed "Check picks does nothing" (it was self-DOSing the rate limit).** The 2026-06-19 b985c2e change made the DEFAULT "Check picks" block-fill the book inline; combined with the per-item trade-search fallbacks, a cold multi-item paste bursts the shared queue past the IP limit (5 req/15s) and trips an ~8-min lockout → everything returns NOT FOUND ("doesn't do shit"). Fix in `fetchRunePrices` (`server.js`): (1) the inline book-fill is now **forceFresh-only** ("Fetch fresh" = explicit, bounded wait); the default never block-fills. (2) The default path NEVER calls `getTradePrice` (the per-item trade search) — that was the other burst source; gated both the unmatched-item search and the currency low-volume search behind `forceFresh`. (3) Un-booked non-skill items on the default path now show **"pricing…"** (instant) instead of NOT FOUND, and the existing gentle fire-and-forget background fill (`refreshRuneBook(stale)`, queue-paced) books them for the next check. The fill only targets real exchange-catalog items, so a genuinely off-exchange paste just stays "pricing…" harmlessly (no wasted calls); "Fetch fresh" remains the authoritative NOT FOUND via item-search. (Dropped a catalog-based pricing…/NOT-FOUND discriminator — `getExchangeCatalog` only loads partially while rate-limited, so it falsely said NOT FOUND; always-"pricing…" on default is simpler and robust.) **Verified live, full cycle:** cold Check picks of Desert Rune/Essence/Medved's Saga → instant "pricing…" (0.1s, zero queue calls even while limited) → gentle background fill populated the book in ~24s → second check priced all three (4/2/1 ex) → trade-status still `limited:false` (no burst). The recurring NOT-FOUND reports (Thrud's/Astrid's/Medved's) are all resolved by this — they were booked-able items that just needed the non-bursting fill. Timing: warm book = instant; first check of new items = instant "pricing…" then ~15-30s for the fill. smoke 90/90.
- 2026-06-21: **Rune Picker — fixed NOT FOUND on names with OCR/paste-corrupted apostrophes.** User pasted `Thane Girťs Rune of Wildness` etc. → NOT FOUND, while `Thane Myrk's Rune of Summer` (clean apostrophe) priced. Confirmed via `/api/trade2/data/static` that all four ARE real exchange runes (catalog has `Thane Girt's Rune of Wildness`…). Root cause: OCR/odd copy-paste turns an apostrophe+letter (`t'`) into a single caron letter (`ť`/`ľ`/`ď`); `normalizeName` had no diacritic handling, so `ť` fell into the `[^a-z0-9]` catch-all and became a SPACE (`girťs`→`gir s`), never matching the catalog key `girts`. Fix: prepend `.normalize("NFD").replace(/[̀-ͯ]/g,"")` to `normalizeName` — decomposes `ť`→`t`+combining-caron and drops the mark, so `Girťs`→`girts` matches `Girt's`→`girts` (the lost apostrophe is stripped anyway). Safe/strictly-more-robust: only touches accented chars (also fixes legit accents é→e), no effect on ASCII names. (`lx`→`1x` quantity was already handled by stripQuantity's `[0-9Il|l]` class.) Live-verified: the exact corrupted 4-line paste through Fetch fresh now prices all four (15/15/10/1 ex) and displays the clean catalog names. smoke 90/90.
- 2026-06-21: **New tool — Filter Helper** (`#filter-helper`). Finds Currency-Exchange items worth keeping that a loot filter (NeverSink/custom) might hide, and emits a top-priority **Show** block to paste at the TOP of the filter (first-match-wins → never hidden; non-destructive, no filter parsing). Two-stage so we never scan dead markets: **(1)** poe.ninja PoE2 trade VOLUME gates candidates to liquid items (`volumePrimaryValue`; endpoint `https://poe.ninja/poe2/api/economy/exchange/current/overview?league=&type=<RUNE_CATEGORIES.type>`, `items[]` id→name + `lines[]`). **This is the user-approved NARROW poe.ninja exception (volume-only, NEVER a displayed price) — see memory [[no-poe-ninja-ever]]; delete the whole poe.ninja path when GGG `service:cxapi` lands** (cxapi returns traded volume + all prices in one call, making both poe.ninja AND the scan obsolete). All `// ponytail: poe.ninja TEMP` marked. **(2)** survivors (vol ≥ minVol AND poe.ninja val ≥ minEx×0.5, generous floor) are PRICE-CONFIRMED on OUR Trade2 exchange — the only price shown. **Rate-limit lesson (again):** pricing ~60 candidates = ~21 exchange calls; an 8s/call gap TRIPPED the IP limit (90/8≈11 > the 10-per-90s rule), so the scan paces at **10s/call** (`buildFilterHelper`, ~3-4 min) and writes the cache **progressively** (items appear as it runs; a partial trip saves progress + shows "partial — click Refresh to finish"). Background single-flight (`getFilterHelper` returns cache + `building` flag, never blocks); front end (`filter-helper.js`) polls every 8s while building, has a Copy button + live rate-limit countdown. Cached 6h (`.filter-helper.json`, gitignored). Server: `GET /api/filter-helper?league=&minEx=1&minVol=10&refresh=1`. Files: `filter-helper.{js,css}` (scoped `.toolroot-fh`, reuses the shared `.pagehead/.controls/.status/.tablewrap/table` baseline), wired into index (nav + view + link + script). Live-verified end-to-end: poe.ninja gate → 62 liquid candidates → gentle scan → 16 items ≥1ex (Fracturing Orb 1199, Origin Cradle 1111, Divine 268, Annulment 200, fragments/breach/vaal orbs …) + correct Show block; screenshot-confirmed UI. smoke 90/90. Scope is exchange-priceable items only; rare GEAR bases are out (no price source — value is roll-dependent).
- 2026-06-21: **Filter Helper — optional filter-aware pruning** (`filter-helper.js`, client-side). User: the Show block listed everything ≥1ex incl. items the filter already shows. Added a "paste your loot filter" box (`#fhFilter`, in a `<details>`); the filter NEVER leaves the browser — `parseFilter()` extracts the Show/Hide BaseType sets and the list is pruned to **`inHide ∧ ¬inShow`** (the items the filter actually hides), then the Show block is rebuilt client-side from just those. Pruning is instant + reuses the cached server scan (so we don't re-scan; the ~3-min scan is one-time/shared). Cascade handling for NeverSink's tiered structure (Show S→D, then Hide tiers + a big `exhide` "hide all known low" block, then a `restex` catch-all): an item is hidden iff it's in a Hide BaseType list and NOT in any Show list (Show wins first-match). **Leveling nuance handled:** blocks with `AreaLevel <= N` and no `AreaLevel >=` are leveling-only and ignored (e.g. Regal Orb is *shown* while leveling but *hidden* in maps → correctly flagged hidden). Verified the parser against the user's real NeverSink 4-Very-Strict filter: all valuable items (Divine/Fracturing/Greater Exalted/Orb of Alchemy/the **Thane runes** at tiers B/C) correctly read as SHOWN (not hidden); Regal Orb/Orb of Transmutation/Greater Orb of Transmutation correctly HIDDEN. **Key finding:** at ≥1ex, NeverSink 4-Very-Strict already shows ~everything valuable — so with a filter pasted the tool honestly reports "your filter already shows all N valuable items — nothing to unhide" and surfaces only the genuinely-hidden tail. Known gaps (minor): exact base-name match only (the `restex` partial/prefix catch-alls and Class-only gear hides aren't simulated — fine, exchange items are all BaseType-matched; gear is out of scope). smoke 90/90; screenshot-confirmed pruning (1 of 16 hidden → Show block rebuilt to that one).
- 2026-06-21: **Filter Helper — scope the SCAN by the filter (server-side), not just the display.** The full ~62-item liquid scan kept tripping the shared rate limit even at a 10s/call gap, because the 10s only spaces the scan's OWN calls — the currency strip / economy / rune-book calls slot into the gaps and the combined rate trips it (the shared queue uses a fixed min-gap, not a sliding-window limiter). Fix: when a filter is pasted, the client now POSTs the **hidden base set** (the filter's `hide ∧ ¬show` names, from `parseFilter`) and `buildFilterHelper(league,minEx,minVol,hiddenSet)` filters the liquid candidates to `liquid ∩ hidden` **before** scanning — usually a handful (often ~0 for a strict filter ≥1ex), so the scan is too small to meaningfully add to a trip. Endpoint now accepts **POST `{league,minEx,minVol,hidden:[...],refresh}`** (GET = the old full liquid scan, the heavy/risky path — use a filter to keep it light); `getFilterHelper`/cache keyed by `hiddenSig` (= hidden-set size). Client moved pruning from post-display to a pre-scan input: filter paste/edit debounce-re-scans (1.5s), result is server-filtered (`d.filtered`, `d.liquidTotal`), removed the client-side `buildShowBlock` (server builds it). Verified: syntax, parser unit test, smoke 90/90, POST path returns `filtered:true`. NOT yet verified live end-to-end (dev server was rate-limited from earlier full scans when I tried) — the scoped scan is tiny by construction, but confirm `liquid ∩ hidden` prices correctly + doesn't trip on a fresh run. TODO maybe: give the SHARED queue a real sliding-window limiter (≤5/15s, ≤10/90s, ≤30/300s) so NO tool combo can trip it — would retire all these per-tool gentle-scan hacks (and is moot once cxapi lands).
- 2026-06-21: **Filter Helper — REDESIGNED so it can no longer trip the shared rate limit (supersedes the per-tool gentle-scan hacks above).** User: "it keeps limiting itself." Root cause was never just the burst — the scan **auto-ran on every page-open and filter-edit** (`getFilterHelper` rebuilt on staleness) and re-fired the instant the limit cleared = a self-perpetuating loop; the old `fetchExchangeChunked` **backfill** also turned each "1-call" group into up to 4 (high-value items have empty exalted-side offers → every one "starved" → re-fetched). New architecture: **(1) Price book, scanned once** — `buildFilterHelperBook(league,minVol,scan)` prices the full liquid candidate set and caches it to `.filter-helper.json` (`{league,minVol,prices:[{id,name,ex,volume,category}],partial,updated}`), independent of minEx/the filter. **(2) Serve = pure in-memory** — `serveFilterHelper(book,minEx,filterSpec)` applies minEx + filter scoping with ZERO Trade2 calls, so opens/filter-edits/polls never touch the limit (proven: identical `queue.lastCall` across repeated opens). **(3) Scan only on explicit Generate** — `getFilterHelper` kicks the network scan ONLY when `force` (refresh=1) AND not limited; a cold first-open kicks a **cache-seed** (`scan=false`, no calls). The seed pulls instant prices from the warm currency-rates cache + Rune Picker book + economy divine-side cache (match by id AND normalized NAME — the currency cache and static catalog assign DIFFERENT ids to the same item, so id-only missed almost everything). The live scan uses the **raw batched exchange call (no backfill)**, 3 ids/call, ≥10s gap, **stops dead if limited, never auto-retries**, progressive save. Endpoint: GET/POST `/api/filter-helper` (POST body `{league,minEx,minVol,filter:{shownBases,shownClasses,hiddenBases,hiddenClasses,catchAllHide},refresh}`; `limited` is informational only now). **Filter scoping also fixed**: "hidden" now = a candidate the filter does NOT *show* (Show wins; `Class` rules now parsed, not just `BaseType`; catch-all `Hide` = "hide everything not shown") — old logic only matched explicit `Hide BaseType` and silently full-scanned when none were found. Server exports `buildFilterSpec`/`filterHelperHides`; offline unit test `filter-helper-test.js` (wired into smoke). Live-verified end-to-end on a fresh server: open seeds 3 cached items with 0 exchange calls; Generate paced a live scan with `limited=False` throughout (queue was at its 30s adaptive max from prior testing — even gentler than the 10s floor), progressively pricing the special items a filter hides (Breachlord Sac 50, Architect's Orb 10, Orb of Extraction 10, Core Destabiliser 5, …). smoke 91/91. KNOWN: divine-side items (omens, Hinekora's, Mirror) are priced only if the economy divine cache has them seeded — the exalted-side scan won't price them (follow-up: price the `need` set's high-value/zero-exalted items via `divineMarketPrice`). Basic currency (Chaos/Vaal/Alch) aren't candidates (pre-existing ninja/catalog resolution gap) but that's fine — every filter shows them via `Class "Currency"`. Pre-existing latent bug noticed: `resolveArbitrageItems` swallows a rate-limited static-catalog fetch and caches an EMPTY catalog for 1h (cold+limited → 0 candidates app-wide); worth persisting the static catalog to disk.

- 2026-06-22: **TABLET MOD VALUE research (live Trade2) — finding: single tablet mods are LOW-value.** Real tablet category = `map.tablet`; mods are explicit stats (ids via `data/stats`). KEY: ranking by roll-ceiling is misleading — the high-rolling mods (Essences/Summoning Circle/Shrines %chance ~80-98%) are GENERIC filler on every tablet and are worthless; the valuable CHASE mods are mechanic-specific and roll LOW (Hiveblood qty, extra Hiveborn waves, Wombgift for Breach; extra Vaal Beacon Crystal for Temple; additional Abyss; Tribute for Ritual; etc.). - 2026-06-22: **Rate-limit root cause — NOT per-call pacing; it's SHARED-IP CONTENTION.** GGG `trade-search-request-limit` IP rule = `[5/10s, 15/60s, 30/300s]` → the binding cap is **30 searches per 5 min (~1 per 10s sustained)**. But a sweep tripped a 429 with the queue's own state at only `9/30` in 300s and `3/15` in 60s — i.e. WELL under limit. Means other traffic on the same public IP (the Docker prod app's `warmExchange` every ~2 min + live browser/LAN users) is eating the IP's GGG budget concurrently. **Bulk Trade2 sweeps from the dev box are not viable while prod is live** — no headroom to reserve. Use tiny spaced batches when prod is quiet, or run the sweep ON the prod server through its own queue. (Also: NEVER raw-curl — even `data/filters`/`items`/`stats` are limited; route everything through `trade-queue.js`, already added as a hard rule above.)
- 2026-06-22: **TABLET VALUE — corrected via a HIGH-END sweep (the "single mods ≈1ex" finding was floor-biased and wrong).** User: "tablets aren't worth nothing — sweep the high end, which sell >20ex, don't look at the floor." Probed `map.tablet` with a `trade_filters.price={option:"exalted",min:N}` floor at N=20/100/300 (throwaway queue script, spaced, deleted). Findings: **tablets are saturated with listings at every tier up to 300ex+** — well-rolled / multi-mod tablets routinely command 100–300ex. The old conclusion measured the cheapest listing per mod (always 1ex) and missed this. The value driver is **desirable mod COMBINATIONS**, and these mods recur across the expensive tier: (a) content-agnostic — **Strongbox chance, Summoning Circle chance, Essence chance, Gold found, additional Rare Chests**; (b) per-mechanic chase — Breach **Hiveblood** / Unstable Breaches; Abyss **Desecrated Currency** / additional Abysses / Pit-reward / per-closed-Pit Effectiveness; Delirium **Unique Boss** / Simulacrum Splinter stack / fog-never-dissipates; Ritual **Tribute** / Reroll Favours; Temple (base = **Temple Tablet**) extra **Crystal** from Vaal Beacons. **Wording is now CONFIRMED from live listing text** (was best-effort guesses) — updated `waystone-data.js`: removed unconfirmed tokens (Wombgift/Hive Blood/abyssal-pit/abyssal-modifier), added the confirmed chase tokens per content, added the 5 high-value generic mods to `tabletGeneral`, fixed Temple `tabletToken` "aal|emple"→"emple". **Removed Expedition content type entirely** (user: Expedition tablets aren't in 0.5 — they don't exist). smoke 93/93 (updated the Breach tablet-regex check `ombgift`→`iveblood`). KNOWN: per-mod ex attribution still isn't isolated (a 300ex tablet has 4 mods + possible corruption — can't credit one mod); a real per-tablet value model would need item-search by stat hash. Bases seen but not modelled as content types: **Overseer Tablet** (Map-Boss farming: boss item-qty / boss modifiers / boss waystone-drops) — add if the user wants boss-tablet chips. New base wording still worth a final in-stash glance, but it's grounded in live trade text now, not guessed.
- 2026-06-22: **Tablet Mod Value table built** (user: "so there's no mod value for tablets? build it"). Tablets are MULTI-MOD so a per-mod ex curve (waystone-style) misleads — instead the model samples `map.tablet` at price FLOORS (≥1/≥100/≥300ex) and tiers each known mod by the **highest floor it appears on** (High ≥300 · Mid ≥100 · Low <100), with a sample count. Honest signal = "appears on expensive tablets", NOT the mod priced in isolation (a 300ex tablet has 4 mods). **Server** (`server.js`): `sampleTablets(league)` + `tabletSampleAt` (category `map.tablet`, `trade_filters.price={option:exalted,min}`, sort asc — asc is invalid WITHOUT a price filter, desc returns fake 99999999 walls; fetch caps at 10 ids, spread across depth for variety); `.tablet-weights.json` cache + 2-min cooldown; endpoints `GET /api/tablet/market-weights` (read cache) + `POST /api/tablet/market-weights/refresh` (sweep, ~6 calls, mirrors the waystone refresh incl. graceful `limited`). **Data** (`waystone-data.js`): baked `tabletSamples` (real tablets from the 2026-06-22 high-end probe at ≥1/20/100/300ex) so the table works offline. **Front end** (`map-juicer.js`/`.css`): `#mjAside` split into two slots — "Waystone Mod Value" (renamed) + new "Tablet Mod Value" card; `renderTabletValue()` regex-matches each `tabletGeneral`+per-content `desirable` token against the sample texts, ranks by tier then count, tier badges (good/mid/bad) + "Refresh from market" button. smoke **94/94** (+1: tablet table ranks mods into tiers, a chase mod reads High). **NOT live-verified end-to-end:** the live `refresh` sweep is blocked RIGHT NOW by shared-IP contention with prod (queue's own state `1/12` yet `limited` for ~590s — confirms line below) — the endpoint ran and handled the limit cleanly, and the table is seeded from real probe data; click "Refresh from market" when the IP is quiet (or run on prod) to populate live + drop the `baked` badge. Per-mod ex still isn't isolatable (multi-mod tablets) — tiers are the honest ceiling.

- 2026-06-22: **Rate-limit discipline written down — `RATE-LIMITS.md`** (user: "you keep doing this everytime i run you"). New repo file is a hard checklist for not tripping the GGG Trade2 limit; `[!important]` pointer added at the TOP of AGENTS.md, and memory `[[rate-limit-discipline]]` + index updated. Core: the IP is SHARED with prod (`warmExchange` every ~2 min) so own-queue state can read under-limit and still 429; the start-of-sequence `tradeStatus()` check is a snapshot, not a promise (trips happen MID-sequence); minimize call COUNT not just spacing (cap loops, stop early, no stacked bursts); route everything through `trade-queue.js` (never raw-curl, incl data/filters|items|stats); on a trip wait the FULL window, don't poll/retry. `/api/trade-status` is a LOCAL read (no GGG call) so checking it to size a wait is free.
- 2026-06-22: **New tool — Tab Tracker** (`#tab-tracker`). Values the currency parked in a public stash tab at live market prices, **Trade2-only, no OAuth/cookie**. PoE2's legacy `character-window/get-stash-items` returns **403 unauthenticated** (tested — public-tab read needs a session), so instead: the user makes ONE tab public and prices every item in it at a **10-divine SENTINEL**; `fetchTrackedTab(account,league)` (server.js) searches Trade2 by account (`trade_filters.filters.account.input`, sort price DESC), fetches listings in chunks, keeps only the `==10 divine` block (genuine high sales sort above it, cheaper sales below → early-stop once out of the block), builds `"Name xStack"` lines, and reuses **`fetchRunePrices(…, forceFresh=false)`** to value them off the existing exchange book. Endpoint `GET /api/tab-tracker?account=&league=`. Files: `tab-tracker.{js,css}` (scoped `.toolroot-tt`, reuses the shared `.pagehead/.controls/.status/.tablewrap/table` baseline + a div/ex total banner), wired into index (nav + view + link + script). smoke **93/94** (the 1 fail = the known-flaky home-currency skeleton timing check; the new view passes the desktop+mobile walks — added to both). **LIVE-VERIFIED the READ end-to-end**: the endpoint returned 30 real tracked items (essences — Greater Essence of Ruin ×28, Perfect Essence of Sorcery ×19, Essence of the Abyss ×10, …) with correct names+stacks; graceful `{limited:true}` on a mid-sweep 429 (no crash). **NOT yet verified live: the populated VALUES/total** — the gentle book-fill for a 30-item tab is itself too big a burst and tripped the shared IP (590s) before prices populated; values fill on later visits as the IP allows (the documented rune-book "accurate on 2nd check" behavior). KNOWN GAPS / follow-ups: (a) **book-fill bursts on large tabs** — a 30-essence fill trips the limit; should page/cap the fill per visit (or fill incrementally) so a big tab doesn't lock the IP; do a final live values+total check when prod is quiet. (b) **sentinel leak** — a genuine sale priced at exactly 10 div is picked up too (saw a "Lapis Amulet" in the block); user reserves 10 div for tracking, accepted (ponytail comment in code). (c) sentinel/league are hardcoded conventions; account is a UI input.
- 2026-06-22: **Tab Tracker — cached read + capped incremental valuation (fixes the rate-limit trips)** (user: "cant you just search trades by me at 10 div"). The READ was never the problem (~4 calls, fine); the TRIP was the VALUATION — `fetchRunePrices`' background fill handed all 30+ essences to `fetchExchangeChunked` in one go (`EXCHANGE_BATCH_CAP=3` → ~10-call burst). Rebuilt `fetchTrackedTab`: (1) **cache the tab contents** to `.tab-tracker.json` (gitignored, 10-min TTL, keyed account+league) via `readTrackedTabListings` — so re-pricing visits skip the search/fetch entirely; `refresh=1` forces a re-read. (2) **Price directly from the rune/exchange book** (no `fetchRunePrices`), and **cap the fill to `TAB_FILL_PER_VISIT=6` unbooked items/visit** (≤2 exchange calls — can't burst), bounded by `RUNE_FRESH_DEADLINE_MS`; the rest stay "pricing…" and fill on the next (cheap, cached) visit. Returns `pricedCount`/`remaining`/`limited`. Front-end (`tab-tracker.js`) forces a fresh read then **auto-polls the cached path every 6s**, filling a batch each time until `remaining==0` or `limited` (then "click Value tab again to finish"). Endpoint takes `&refresh=1`. **LIVE-VERIFIED**: fresh read → 56 items, priced 6, real partial total **1.18 div / 353 ex**, `limited=false`; cache hit on the next visit (no re-search). smoke **94/94**. HONEST CAVEAT: under heavy shared-IP contention with prod even a 2-call fill can trip (saw it on the 2nd batch) — the tool now **degrades gracefully** (partial total + resume later) instead of crashing/locking out, but full population still needs prod-quiet headroom. The real cure remains the shared sliding-window limiter (see [RATE-LIMITS.md](RATE-LIMITS.md)). Possible knobs if still trippy: lower `TAB_FILL_PER_VISIT`, widen the poll interval. NOTE: the user's literal "search by me at 10 div" price-filter (`trade_filters.filters.price`) wasn't wired — the desc-sort + sentinel-block read already works; test the price filter live and switch only if it cleanly returns exactly the 10-div listings.

- 2026-06-22: **Regex Forge FIXED — the waystone tokens were broken; grounded them in a live stash tooltip** (user: "the regex thing doesnt really work" + screenshot of a Tier-15 waystone). Real in-stash labels (confirmed from the screenshot): `Item Rarity: +X%`, `Pack Size: +X%`, `Monster Rarity: +X%`, `Monster Effectiveness: +X%`, `Waystone Drop Chance: +X%`, and a red `Corrupted` line. The old `tokens.line` bridges were wrong: `packSize:"m.+e:"` matched NO real label (Pack Size has no "m"), `magicMonsters`/`rareMonsters` didn't correspond to the actual Monster Rarity/Effectiveness labels, and the greedy `i.+ty:` `.+` could stretch to match the WRONG stat (Monster Rarity instead of Item Rarity). Rewrote `waystone-data.js tokens.line` to literal label substrings (`"item rarity"`, `"pack size"`, `"monster rarity"`, `"monster effectiveness"`, `"drop chance"` — "drop chance" handles the hidden word in "Waystone Drop **Chance**:") + added `tokens.corrupted`. `map-juicer.js`: replaced `tens`/`atLeast` with `geNum(pct)` → `Label: \+([d-9][0-9]|[0-9][0-9][0-9])%` (uses `[0-9]` not `.` so it can't eat the trailing `%`; bridges the real "Label: +X%" format). Output now e.g. `"(item rarity: \+([6-9][0-9]|[0-9][0-9][0-9])%|pack size: \+([3-9][0-9]|[0-9][0-9][0-9])%)"`. **Added a "Corrupted only" toggle** (`wCorrupt` → appends `"corrupted"` block) per user. Updated the 3 smoke forge assertions to the new format + added a corrupted-toggle check. smoke 94/94 (1 intermittent home-skeleton flake). The waystone label wording is now CONFIRMED from a live tooltip (was the long-standing "verify in a live stash" TODO); a real in-game highlight test of the generated regex is still the final nice-to-have.

- 2026-06-22: **smoke-test hardened — browser suite no longer crashes under rate-limit throttle + the home-skeleton flake is fixed (now a stable 95/95).** Two root causes of the recurring "smoke browser suite is red" pain: (1) the desktop-walk + mobile `#home` navigations used `waitUntil:"networkidle"` and were UNMOCKED, so a throttled IP kept the currency fetch pending past 30s → goto TimeoutError → **uncaught** (browserChecks has only `finally`, main didn't catch) → the whole run crashed before the summary/exit code. - 2026-06-23: **Tab Tracker — RESUMABLE per-band read (clicking again no longer restarts).** Real failure the user hit: a ~136+ item read tripped mid-way, and clicking "Value tab" again RE-READ from scratch and re-tripped at the same spot → never finished. - 2026-06-23: **Tab Tracker — hands-off auto-resume read.** Even on the dedicated Nord IP, a big read (119+ items ≈ 15 calls) busts GGG's short window (~15/60s) and trips — that's inherent to ONE IP's budget, VPN or not; the VPN's win is only removing the user's game traffic from the budget, not enlarging it. So instead of "click Value tab again" per cooldown, the read now **auto-resumes**: on a trip it polls the free local `/api/trade-status`, shows a countdown ("auto-resuming in Ns…"), waits the cooldown, and continues the unread bands until done — one click, walk away. - 2026-06-23: **Filter Helper — gutted the pricing/Trade2 scan; it's now a pure client-side "what currency does my filter HIDE" linter.** User: "scrap the trade part… can it not properly see what's hidden?" The old tool was mostly a price engine (poe.ninja volume gate + Trade2 exchange scan) that hung/rate-limited, and its hide-detection was order-BLIND (a set-based `filterHelperHides` couldn't see a Hide sitting *above* a currency Show). Rewrite: `filter-helper.js` now parses the pasted `.filter` into ordered blocks and **simulates the real first-match-wins cascade** (`parseFilterBlocks`/`blockMatches`/`verdictFor`/`analyzeFilter`) over PoE2's actual currency item-classes — confirmed against a real filter: **Stackable Currency** (covers orbs/shards/essences/runes/soul cores/catalysts/distilled/splinters — all that one class, addressed by BaseType), plus **Omen / Tablet / Breachstones / Map Fragments** as their own classes. Per-group it reports shown vs **HIDDEN** + the deciding line, names the valuable orbs that are hidden, and builds a top-of-filter Show block (whole hidden classes by Class + loose bases by BaseType). AND-within-a-block honored (`Class X + BaseType Y` hides only Y, not all of X); leveling-only blocks (`AreaLevel <=` no floor) ignored; `Continue` handled. 100% in-browser — **no server, no Trade2, no rate limits, ever**. - 2026-06-23: **Tab Tracker — prices off the BID (sell value), marks no-buyer items, and RANKS the tab by what's worth selling.** User reported essences valued way too high (Essence of Battle "5 ex" when the real exchange ratio is 1 exalted : 5 essence = 0.2 ex). Root cause: the shared exchange book (`refreshRuneBook`, used by Tab Tracker `valueTabItems` AND Rune Picker) priced off the cheapest standing ASK, which for thin currency is an aspirational single far above reality — the failure `server.js:1294` documents for illiquid orbs (which the curated cheap currencies already avoid via two-sided `geoMidRate`). Fix: `refreshRuneBook` now fetches both legs (ask + bid, batched like the arbitrage scan) and prices each item off the **robust BID** (`robustBidPx`, mirrors geoMidRate's bid logic) = what buyers actually pay. When **no buyer stands** on the exchange, the item is marked `{thin:true}` and shown as **"no live buyers"** (no fake price). Tab Tracker then **ranks results by firm sell value desc** — sellable on top, no-buyer items dimmed at the bottom; header "<x> ex sellable · n/m priced · k no buyers". **Deliberately does NOT show the cheapest-ask as an "indicative" number** for no-buyer items: tested live and the ask side is ~100x noise (Battle "lists" ~20 ex but sells ~0.2), which ranked worthless essences at #1 — the exact inflated-number problem this started from (ask kept only as a hidden sub-sort hint). **KEY DOMAIN FACT (verified live): the PoE2 Currency Exchange currently has NO standing buy offers for essences** (battle/body/electricity/sorcery + Iron Rune, Soul Core of Zalatl all thin), so essence-heavy tabs show mostly "no buyers"; items WITH bids price fine (Soul Core of Tacati 10 ex, Desert Rune 5 ex). For real essence numbers, hand-curation (like the tablet mods) is the only route — the live exchange lacks the data. Shared book → Rune Picker now also uses bid (sell value); thin items fall through to NOT FOUND there. Verified end-to-end via paste mode + in-browser (correct ranking, dimmed no-buyer rows, poll completes, 0 console errors); smoke 95/0.
- 2026-06-24: **Home page reworked — chaos is now the base currency + the marketing hero is gone.** (1) Base unit exalts → **Chaos Orb** on the home page only: the currency strip, economy headline/cards now read in chaos (`home.js` converts the exalted-denominated rates via the live chaos rate; `server.js economyCurrent` now carries `chaosEx` so the economy `current` point can convert — other tools still price in ex). Home is now: Trade2 pill → currency prices → economy trend. Dead `.hero`/`.stat`/`.eyebrow`/`.lead` CSS removed. Smoke 96/0 (added chaos-base + trade-pill checks); screenshot-verified.
- 2026-06-24: **Dump filter CORRECTED — waystone value is combination-driven, not per-stat (user was right).** Earlier per-stat "best-stat ≤Nex" model was wrong: a deeper buy-side sweep GATED on the real class (corrupted + 0 revives, via `map_revives max 0` + `misc_filters.corrupted`) showed the WHOLE juiced-corrupted class is ~5ex bulk **even at high single rolls** (Monster Rarity ≥75 alone = 1-5ex; Drop ≥110 alone = 1ex) — the in-game price-check massively over-states these (user confirmed a "40-70ex" map sold for **5ex instantly**). Only two things break past 5ex: **(a) Item Rarity ≥60%** (~50-180ex, scarce; ≥70% doesn't exist on market) and **(b) high-roll COMBOS** — `monrar≥70 + drop≥100 + pack≥25` sampled at **25/100/400ex** (only ~3 on the whole market; this is the user's "2 div" Cruel Stone). New `buildDump` (map-juicer.js) drops the cap/curve logic and keeps the empirical money signals: **Item Rarity ≥{dumpRarityKeep=60}% OR Drop Chance ≥100% OR Monster Rarity ≥100%**, dumps the rest. Drop ≥100% doubles as the user's keep-rule ("don't trash anything above 100%" — sustain value) and the combo signal (all valuable combos carry it). Stepper now tunes the rarity-keep % (40-70). Live regex (137/250): `"corrupted" "revives available: 0" "!item rarity: \+[6-9][0-9]%" "!drop chance: \+[0-9][0-9][0-9]%" "!monster rarity: \+[0-9][0-9][0-9]%"`. waystone-data itemRarity curve updated to the step-function reality (≤55%≈5ex, ≥60%→50-180ex, ceiling 66). **Lesson: gate market probes on the actual item class, and never trust the in-game price-check for multi-mod items.** Smoke 101/0.
- 2026-06-24 [SUPERSEDED by the entry above]: **Dump filter tuned to 5ex + value-cap stepper + buy-side re-probe of the ignored waystone mods.** (1) Dump cutoff default is now **5 ex** (was 40) with a **stepper** (5–100 ex, ±5) in the dump panel — `dumpCap` in map-juicer.js. (2) `geNum` is ceiling-aware: stats that can't roll 3 digits drop the `|[0-9][0-9][0-9]` alt, keeping the multi-exclusion regex well under 250. (3) **Buy-side Trade2 probe (2026-06-24, cheapest-ask Tier-16, through the queue)** of the mods we'd dismissed/omitted: enumerated `data/filters` → the full waystone map_filters are tier/packsize/magic_monsters(=Effectiveness)/iir/rare_monsters/revives/**bonus(=Drop Chance)**/**gold**/**experience**. Findings baked into `waystone-data.js`: **Drop Chance is worthless to BUY** (~1ex even at 105% — was a too-high est of 22; sustain isn't paid for), **Monster Rarity is a mild ~5ex at ≥60%** (was "worthless ~1ex"), and **Waystone Gold / Experience have no liquid buy market** (0 listings at modest rolls) so they stay unpriced. Net effect on the 5ex dump regex: drops the Drop-Chance exclusion, adds Monster Rarity ≥60%. Live output (183/250): `"corrupted" "revives available: 0" "!item rarity: \+[3-9][0-9]%" "!pack size: \+[2-9][0-9]%" "!monster effectiveness: \+[2-9][0-9]%" "!monster rarity: \+([6-9][0-9]|[0-9][0-9][0-9])%"`. Smoke 101/0.
- 2026-06-24: **Regex Forge — defaults start empty + new "Low-value dump" waystone mode.** (1) Forge now opens with nothing set (rarity/pack floors 0, all toggles off, tablet content no longer auto-ticks its mods) so you build up instead of deleting every time. (2) New third waystone match-mode **"Low-value dump"** (`map-juicer.js` `buildDump`): finds corrupted + fully-juiced (0 revives) waystones worth roughly **under 40 ex** — the cheap slammed maps safe to vendor. It requires `"corrupted"` + `"revives available: 0"` and excludes any reward stat rolled into its ≥40ex band. **Thresholds are derived at runtime from the baked `marketWeights` curves** (`dumpThreshold` floors the 40ex crossing to a 10% decade, conservatively) — NO live scan, NO refresh button, re-derives only if the Mod Value table is re-swept (e.g. a major patch). With current curves: excludes Item Rarity ≥50% and Pack Size ≥40%; Effectiveness/Drop/Monster-Rarity peak under 40ex so they get no exclusion. Output verified live: `"corrupted" "revives available: 0" "!item rarity: \+([5-9][0-9]|[0-9][0-9][0-9])%" "!pack size: \+([4-9][0-9]|[0-9][0-9][0-9])%"` (128/250). Caveat: value ≈ best stat (the tool's model), so a map with several mid rolls may total higher — spot-check. Smoke 100/0.

- 2026-06-24: **Rune Picker — ask-side floor for real-value runes (fixes the "of Aldur" no-buyers bug), `RUNE_BOOK_VERSION`→8.** User reported Betrayal/Ire/Passion/Breath of Aldur all showing "no buyers" — impossible, they clearly sell. Live-probed the exchange: all four are in the `data/static` Runes catalog and have **14–35 real ask-side sellers but ZERO bulk bids**, so the pure bid-only book (v7) marked every one `thin` → "no buyers". Fix (`refreshRuneBook`, server.js): when there's no bid but `cheapestAsk` returns **≥2 ex/item AND ≥3 sellers above par** (new `aboveParCount` on `cheapestAsk`), price off the lowest ask as `side:"ask"` — UI shows source "trade2 exchange (ask)" + "lowest ask — sell-side floor", confidence capped **low** (`bookResultFor`). The ≥2ex gate is the guard: cheap spam (Greater Storm/Iron/Storm Rune) floors at par 1ex → fails → still "no buyers" (re-verified live after the fix). Tried `aboveParCount≥3` alone first — it FAILED because overpriced 2:1/3:1 spam clears it; the cheapest-ask-≥2ex test is the true discriminator. Live results: Betrayal 10ex / Ire 5ex / Passion 5ex / Breath 20ex (off real asks); GSR/Iron/Storm still "no buyers". The Picker did NOT need a rebuild — OCR + flow are fine; this was one wrong pricing rule. Smoke 107/0.
