- 2026-06-24: **Rune Picker — fixed high-value/chase items reading "no buyers" (Cadigan's Epiphany, Celestial Alloy, Astrid's Creativity), `RUNE_BOOK_VERSION`→9.** Follow-on to the Aldur-rune fix. User pasted a 500ex+ chase unique-rune and got "no buyers". Live-probed: all are in the exchange catalog, but three compounding bugs hid them — (1) book read `status:"online"` only → chase items (sellers usually offline) returned ZERO offers; switched the book's both legs to `status:"any"`. (2) the ask logic over-filtered — replaced the `stock≥2` skip + `aboveParCount≥3` gate (both killed thin chase items) with: drop par/sub-par spam (`px≤1`), de-bait (drop a lone ask <½ the next — Cadigan's had a 1ex bait under a 4444ex wall), then gate `px≥2`. (3) **page-cap starvation** — the exchange caps responses at ~100 listings TOTAL and Greater Storm Rune's 1ex spam ate 99/100, starving everything else to zero in a shared batch; so the Rune Picker now fetches the **ask leg per-item** (`refreshRuneBook(…,{perItemAsk:true})`, ask `batchCap=1`) while Tab Tracker keeps the batched read. Verified live in one mixed paste incl. the spam whale: Cadigan 4444 / Astrid 13 / Celestial 10 / Betrayal 2 / Ire 2 ex (all `side:"ask"`, low-conf), Greater Storm Rune still "no buyers". Caveat told to user: 4444 is the lowest *standing* ask (sparse book: a 1ex bait + a 4444 wall), not a confirmed ~500ex sale — exchange is a rough floor for sparse chase items (see [[exchange-book-bid-priced]]). Smoke 107/0, backfill 39/0.
- 2026-06-24: **Rune Picker — item-search fallback for chase items the bulk exchange can't price, `RUNE_BOOK_VERSION`→10.** User: Cadigan's Epiphany (in-game Market Ratio 576:1) read "no buyers". Probed it — the exchange offer book is genuinely a 1ex bait + a 4444ex wall (only 2 standing offers, `total:2`); GGG's 576 comes from matched-trade history the offer-search endpoint doesn't expose. Item-search (`/search`+`/fetch`) shows the real book: cheapest cluster ~1 divine. Fix: `cheapestAsk` returns `depth` (# above-floor sellers); when no bid and the ask book is a thin wall (`depth` 1–3), `refreshRuneBook` (Rune-Picker `perItemAsk` only) calls `getTradePrice` (de-baited + ex-converted) and books `side:"market"` (source "trade2 search", medium conf). BUDGET 2/fill + stop-on-limited because `/search` is on a tighter rate policy than the exchange — a multi-chase paste bursting searches blanked everything (`refreshRuneBook` bailed on the 429); now the rest fall back to the exchange ask. Verified live: Cadigan 310ex (item-search, ≈1 div) / Astrid 13ex (deep book → ask, no search) / Betrayal 2ex / Greater Storm Rune still "no buyers". User CONFIRMED 310ex/≈1div is correct (the "576" was a screenshot misread — no divine-rate bug). Smoke 107/0, backfill 39/0.
- 2026-06-25: **Tab Tracker — one ranged search instead of one-search-per-marker (the "1h for 9 items" fix).** `readTrackedBands` fired a separate Trade2 SEARCH per price marker (default 4-5: 10-14 div). Search is the tight-limit endpoint, so the per-marker burst tripped it → 30-min cooldown → retry → trip → ~an hour. Now: ONE ranged account search (`price.min=minMarker, max=maxMarker`), then sort each result into its band by exact listed price; only a >100-item range (Trade2's per-search result cap) falls back to per-marker to span the cap. **BUT the real volume surprise:** probing the user's account (REDACTED-ACCOUNT, markers 10-14) returned **233 items**, not 9 — the marker read scans the user's WHOLE account for listings in that div range, and round div prices COLLIDE with real sale listings (e.g. `Verisium x34946` at 13div, catalysts, liquid emotions). 233 items = ~24 fetch calls (10/call) = still API-bound even with the ranged search. So the ranged-search fix removes the search-burst (the part that trips fastest) but a genuinely large marker set is inherently slow on the server path; the **browser paste reader** (index.html "Copy reader snippet" → run on pathofexile.com → paste back) is the instant, zero-trade-call path and remains the recommendation for big tabs. Open follow-up: marker COLLISION with real sales inflates the count — suggest the user use uncommon sentinel prices (e.g. 11.1/12.2 div) so only true tracked items match, or scope the read to a single tab if the API exposes tab id. Smoke 63/0, backfill 39/0.
- 2026-06-25: **Tab Tracker — grinds through big tabs hands-off (waits out the 30-min ban).** Follow-up to the ranged-search fix. The scan already auto-resumed across cooldowns, but the front-end (`tab-tracker.js` `waitForCooldown`) bailed at `MAX_AUTO_WAIT=240s` — so a 200+-item tab that hits GGG's 30-min ban (`[30,300,1800]` rule = 30 req/5min → 1800s ban) stopped and required a manual re-click, so it never finished unattended. User: "I don't mind it being slow, just finish on its own (in-game w/ overlay 233 items is <2h)." Fix: `MAX_AUTO_WAIT`→2400 (waits out the 1800s ban + headroom), cycle cap 15→40, countdown shows "Xm Ys" + "leave this open". Safe because the app exits via the gluetun VPN (separate IP from the game client), so an app-side ban doesn't touch in-game trading. A 233-item tab now completes hands-off (~read ~17 calls + price-fill ~3 visits, waiting out a ban if tripped). NOTE: Tab Tracker pricing is batched (does NOT pass `perItemAsk`), so chase items in a tab show "no buyers" rather than the item-search price the Rune Picker now gets — acceptable (tabs are mostly bulk currency/runes); wire `perItemAsk` into `valueTabItems` only if chase-item tab valuation is wanted (costs more calls). Smoke 107/0.
- 2026-06-25: **trade-queue paces PROACTIVELY now (the real "why does it even ban" fix).** User's insight: an in-game overlay reads GGG's rate-limit headers and slows down BEFORE the cap so it never eats the 30-min ban — why don't we? We didn't: `tuneGap` only widened the gap reactively at ≥75% used and capped the wait at 30s. GGG's IP rules are `[5,15,60] [10,90,300] [30,300,1800]` — the `[30,300]` rule needs ~10s/call sustained, but the 30s cap + late reaction blew the budget early → 30-min ban. New `tuneGap`: for each rule, once ≥50% of its budget is used, hold the steady rate `interval/limit` (+12% headroom); brake harder (spread remaining over window) when ≤2 calls left; take the max across rules; single-wait cap raised 30s→120s. Bursts stay fast for small ops (a few calls never reach 50% of any rule), sustained runs auto-throttle to the safe pace. **Simulated vs the real rules**: 3 calls→9s, 8→62s, 32 (a 233-item tab)→~7min, 60→~15min, NONE banned (peaks 24/30, 8/10, 4/5). So big tabs now finish in minutes without ever tripping the long ban. The Tab Tracker UI `MAX_AUTO_WAIT=2400` stays as a backstop for the rare multi-tool simultaneous trip. This touches the SHARED queue (all tools) but is strictly safer (less likely to trip) — aligned with the rate-limit discipline. Smoke 63/0, backfill 39/0.
